    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }

      AppleID.auth.init({

<div id="descriptionContainer">
  
      <div id="description" class="readable stacked" style="right:0">
        
<span id="freeTextContainer14487994516740390832">Sinning never felt so good… A fortuitous encounter. A meeting that should never have happened. <br/><br/>Many years ago, two children from completely different worlds forged a connection, a fateful connection, an unbreakable bond that would change their lives forever… <br/><br/>Salome knows only one way to live—under Prophet David’s rule. In the commune she calls home, Salome knows nothing of</span>
  <span id="freeText14487994516740390832" style="display:none">Sinning never felt so good… A fortuitous encounter. A meeting that should never have happened. <br /><br />Many years ago, two children from completely different worlds forged a connection, a fateful connection, an unbreakable bond that would change their lives forever… <br /><br />Salome knows only one way to live—under Prophet David’s rule. In the commune she calls home, Salome knows nothing of life beyond her strict faith, nor of life beyond the Fence—the fence that cages her, keeps her trapped in an endless cycle of misery. A life she believes she is destined to always lead, until a horrific event sets her free. <br /><br />Fleeing the absolute safety of all she has ever known, Salome is thrust into the world outside, a frightening world full of uncertainty and sin; into the protective arms of a person she believed she would never see again. <br /><br />River ‘Styx’ Nash knows one thing for certain in life—he was born and bred to wear a cut. Raised in a turbulent world of sex, Harleys, and drugs, Styx, unexpectedly has the heavy burden of the Hades Hangmen gavel thrust upon him, and all at the ripe old age of twenty-six—much to his rivals’ delight. <br /><br />Haunted by a crushing speech impediment, Styx quickly learns to deal with his haters. Powerful fists, an iron jaw and the skillful use of his treasured German blade has earned him a fearsome reputation as a man not to be messed with in the shadowy world of outlaw MC’s. A reputation that successfully keeps most people far, far away. <br /><br />Styx has one rule in life—never let anyone get too close. It’s a plan that he has stuck to for years, that is, until a young woman is found injured on his lot… a woman who looks uncannily familiar, a woman who clearly does not belong in his world, yet a woman he feels reluctant to let go…</span>
  <a data-text-id="14487994516740390832" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

      </div>
</div>

I thought about you often, the boy behind the fence, the boy on the outside… the boy who stole my first and only kiss, and I nightly prayed for your safety and happiness. This beautiful, dark, twisted, and exciting book drove me over the edge, and had me losing my shit. I mean really losing my shit, like hyperventilating I even got dizzy. I had to stop at one point and just breathe. Now that is some talented writing. Tillie Cole hats off to you, for writing something that wrung every emotion out of me. I felt everything. <br><br><b>“You were displeased. I was providing you with pleasure. As a woman, that is what is expected of me. It is selfish and a sin to deny you pleasure.” I swallowed back the growl about to let rip from my throat. “Y-you do that a lot wh-where you from? Were you f-forced into that sh-shit?” Hearing the catch of breath, I turned to hear the answer. “It is essential for sharing the Lord’s love, for the sacrificial exchange of bodies. For the leaders of my people… for the men of my people… I… I did not have a choice in this act… None of the sisters did.”-Mae and Styx</b><br><br><a href="http://s327.photobucket.com/user/jessica_hatfield1/media/f05ade1ab1f057602d1a90d0e0211b93_zpstzqbetwu.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">

</a><br><br><b>“I-I just g-got you. I t-tried to stay away, do the right thing. B-because I ain’t no good for you. But fuck, I want you so b-bad I feel like I-I c-can’t breathe. Can’t p-push you away n-no more. Need to have you c-close.”-Styx</b><br><br>Styx was raised in the MC. His dad who died last year was the MC President. Now that job falls on Styx's shoulders at the age of 26. Called the Hangman Mute, because he stutters so bad he can't speak, he had to earn their respect the hard way. 15 years earlier when his father and some others were dumping bodies out in a woods he came across a fenced in area that looked like a prison. There he seen an angel. Wearing weird clothes, crying, she had black hair, beautiful blue wolf like eyes. That day he kissed her through the fence to try to make her happy. For years he had tried to find that place again, he never did , but he never forgot her. So when he finds her 15 years later bleeding to death on his club property, all those old feelings come rushing back. One look and he knows it's her, and he knows he has to protect her. But with an unknown enemy out there and war looming can he keep his Mae safe?<br><br><b>“I have only ever liked one boy in my life. I have only wanted one man to have as my own. I have only ever had one dream since I was eight. Styx, the dream is you. You stole my heart fifteen years ago and you still haven’t given it back.”-Mae</b><br><br>My Styx:<br><br><a href="http://s327.photobucket.com/user/jessica_hatfield1/media/1182e46885fd024b04ab1cb1b4d23bd8_zpsab1ermdg.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1450303344i/17406081._SX540_.jpg" alt=" photo 1182e46885fd024b04ab1cb1b4d23bd8_zpsab1ermdg.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>“I w-want you too. F-fuck, I want you in m-my bed, by my side, on m-my bike. I w-want you as m-my old lady. Taking c-care of me, n-needing me… letting me inside you.”-Styx</b><br><br>Mae was raised in religious commune cult, where their leader, Prophet David, let all the girls ages 8 and up be raped in what was called the lord's sharing. completely shielded from the outside world, and brainwashed since birth by the teachings of the Prophet David, Mae is told that she is to become the 7th wife of Prophet David on her 23rd birthday which will save her people. On the day of her wedding she finds her sister Bella who as been missing for weeks. Bella is dying, locked in a cage where she was raped, whipped and beaten to the point of death. There holding Bella's hand she sees that everything she was taught was wrong, so when Bella dies a few minutes later, she runs. Escaping, but hurt badly Mae ends up passing out in alley and waking up to a new and scary world filled with what looks like evil. Can Mae find her place in this new world that feels so foreign to her. Can she start a life of freedom and love with Styx or will her past come back and drag her home?<br><br><b>“He is everything to me. I see everything in him. We share something no one else can understand.”-Mae</b><br><br>My Mae:<br><br><a href="http://s327.photobucket.com/user/jessica_hatfield1/media/tumblr_lo6nx7H0PK1qc3kzoo1_500_zps1bqs7jxm.png.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">

</a><br><br><b>“Yeah, b-babe, I’m evil. I’ve s-sinned more than you’d b-believe.” I ran my hands down my face. “Truth t-time. I’m bad… p-p-poisoned to my fuckin’ damned s-soul.”-Styx</b><br><br>Omg I loved Styx. He was hard, gitty,and raw. He was a biker through and through. Blood on his hands, but he was good to Mae. Loyal to his men. Totally bad ass with a knife. Styx was sexy as hell! Poor Mae bless her heart. The shit she lived through made me sick. Mae was a fighter, a survivor, and she had a good in her that shined. They didn't break her. She was brave. I loved Mae's character she had such strength. Styx and Mae together were beautiful. Their connection was strong and powerful. Tons of chemistry. Styx was sweet with Mae, gentle. The way he sang and played the guitar for her, and then he taught her to play. So sweet! Mae accepted Styx for him and he was able to relax and just be himself with her. She shined and rediscovered herself with him and he found peace. <br><br><b>“She fell in love with the dark lord, even though it did not seem right, did she not?” I nodded again. Where the hell is she going with this? She sighed happily and blushed. “Just like I have done with you.” I stilled and, putting my hand on her face, thrust her back, catching the blush creeping up her pale cheeks. Was she saying she loved me? Fuck. She was saying she fuckin’ loved me. I slammed my lips to hers and shifted her up on my hardening cock. Against the complaints of others, did he want her to stay by his side too?” Exhaling hard, I replied, “Yeah… yeah, he d-did… a wh-whole fuckin’ lot.” -Mae and Styx</b><br><br><a href="http://s327.photobucket.com/user/jessica_hatfield1/media/couple-motorcycle_zpsswogro94.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">

</a><br><br><b>“What the fuck happened with the skinheads?” Took out seven with my Uzis. Then got caught, carved up. I managed to get my Bowie from my cut, plucked out the last two fuckers’ eyes and made them eat that shit. Then I smashed up their skulls just to be sure, slit throats and stabbed hearts.” “Shit, Styx,” Ky said in a tight voice and swallowed back bile. “You’re one sick motherfucker. Effective, but sick.”-Ky and Styx</b><br><br> I loved the other gang members, especially Flame. There is something wrong with me I know, but I'm just drawn to the broken ones. I wanna fix em I can't help it. And God is Flame 10 kinds of fuckered up. Rider(Cain) I don't know how it happened, but in the course of one book, I went from loving him and feeling sorry for him, to hating him and finding him unredeemable. The shit he pulls, I don't know if I'll ever be able to forgive him. I seen that he get his own book which will be book 4, but Tillie Cole has really got her work cut out for her if she wants me to see good in that man. Especially after he set Pit up, let him be beat, tortured and killed. And he watched it for God sake. And don't even get me started on what he did to Mae and Styx cuzz it makes me want to gut a fictional character. <br><br><b>“I know you think I have betrayed you, but everything was real, Mae. Us, our friendship, everything I said… especially the way I feel about you.” He edged closer to me and I held up my hand, signaling him to stop. He did so. “Really? Was it all real, Rider—Oops! I mean Cain! Forgive me if your kidnapping me and returning me here, to Hell, can be construed as a mere slight against me.”-Cain(Rider) and Mae</b><br><br><a href="http://s327.photobucket.com/user/jessica_hatfield1/media/15499815_zpstb9dvnrx.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1450303344ra/17406084.gif" alt=" photo 15499815_zpstb9dvnrx.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>“Have you ever been part of a Lord’s sharing? Have you ever seen an eight-year-old girl raped, her legs pried apart by a bear trap because she was too scared to understand what was happening to her? Have you ever forced yourself inside a child, Cain, because you believe it will help you get closer to God and because the prophet deemed it so? Well, have you?” He went eerily still. “Well?” I pushed. “Did that happen to you? Here?” he asked through clenched teeth and I frowned, unable to find my words. “Mae! Answer me! Were you… taken as a child… like… that?”-Mae and Cain(Rider)</b><br><br>MC books have to walk a fine line with me. They are either a hit or a miss, because I can't stand cheating or woman beatin', but they can't be sappy pussies either. That is a hard line to walk bad, rule breaker , but not crossing that line into dickhead and this book did it perfectly. This book was amazing. I have never read a book by Tillie Cole before, but after one book I am hooked. I can't wait to see what else she has in store for this series. <br><br><b>“NO! Listen to me, Styx.” I gave her a nod and gripped my hands on her tiny fuckin’ waist. “This is no cage.” Her arms motioned to the clubhouse. “It is freedom. For the first time in my life, I feel wanted… like I finally belong. There is nowhere on Earth I would rather be than here with you. You do not cage me, Styx. You make me soar.”-Mae</b><br><br><a href="http://s327.photobucket.com/user/jessica_hatfield1/media/woman_happy_joy_freedom-copy_zpsz947h7lp.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">

Still, I just need some kind of realism in my books and in my opinion It Ain't Me, Babe reads like a crude fairytale. What bugged me as well were the inconsistencies. Let's talk about the heroine. She's been <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[severely abused and raped her entire life. Maybe when pigs fly.<br><br>The heroine is UNDERNOURISHED, she's thin and very small and yet her tits are so big they <i>spill out over his fingers.</i> Mind you, the hero is six feet four inches tall and weighs 230 pounds. They must be HUGE considering how big his hands are. Yep, Baba makes eyes as big as saucers too. O__O <br><br><b>
  <i>Her eyes were as big as motherfuckin' saucers and her pink lips popped open with a gasp. She didn't speak, just…stared.</i>

My fuckin' woman was braced on the bed, ready to be fucked…Real fucked-up shit!<br>I was wrong.   <i>Then that nose twitched, and my cut covering her naked body fell to the floor, leaving her naked, on offer like a damn platter. Bare-assed naked, perfect curves on show--heavy tits, tight fuckin' frame. Wolf eyes hooded, pink lips moist, ready for me to make her come…for the first time in her bastard life. Begging me with her eyes to make her come so damn hard.<br>"River…" A plea. A breathy, desperate plea slipped from her lips, like she was channelling her inner Marilyn Monroe or something. The voodoo possessive shit took hold of my controls once again.(…)<br><br>"Styx.." she hushed out, riding a small, needy moan. Her nipples were like damn bullets, her hips slowly rocking with need. She drank me in--every cut muscle, shredded arm, bulging vein, every inch of ink. She loved it, creamin' at what she saw. I knew I looked good. That's not arrogance; I worked hard and knew I was cut.</i>
</b><br><br>When I’m reading a book I try to draw a picture of the characters in my mind. I also try to make a connection between the characters, their speech pattern as well as their actions. My problem was that Styx did not feel authentic to me. I get it that biker speech is rough and crude. Although there's no getting round it to point out how extremely limited Styx's vocabulary is. Besides, the way he spoke felt oddly off to me. Was he really that bad-ass guy or did he just try way too hard? It's strange but I couldn't get a handle on the man and his character and I never connected with the MCs emotionally. Frankly, I found the characterizations one-dimensional and perfunctory. <br><br>When I look back at their first real make-out session….geez…Styx acted like an ape beating his chest. King Kong meets <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[abuse victim. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> Yikes. It's nice to know that he stopped in time, though. <br><br>A cheese fest...<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1398875054ra/9475000.gif" alt=" photo oie_301650414mRmMetR_zps908cb069.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Also, getting a character shitfaced, spewing crude language left and right, repeating <i>bitch</i> a thousand times (yes, I got that too, it's biker speech), <b>blowing a fuse all the time,</b> and telling us about the sexcapades don't make for a great biker story, IMO. Plus, letting the <b>cheese seep through the pages</b> doesn’t help one iota to make a book more <i>bad-ass</i> either. Whatever the case may be, the protagonists annoyed me and I found the writing anything but compelling and too clichéd and very repetitive (she was oh-so beautiful and stunningly amazing, her nose twitched one too many times and after a while I've had enough of her wolf eyes). Of course he was beautiful too and the most amazing sight yadda yadda yadda. I was tired of getting their physical features shoved down my throat <b>ad f@cking nauseam.</b> I wanted to end my boredom, so I had to quit.<br><br>James Blunt -- You're Beautiful<br><br><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.youtube.com/watch?v=MK2up_wnxGU">http://www.youtube.com/watch?v=MK2up_...</a><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1398963504ra/9489024.gif" alt=" photo oie_1132210D49n0ryM_zpsf2aafc31.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>On a positive note: I love the cover and I really liked that Styx was disabled. Besides, I did appreciate the author’s effort to include the cult in the storyline. I’m definitely interested in checking out more books that deal with that subject matter in the future. Looking at the big picture, however, the book is not a shiny example and failed big time. Unfortunately it's nowhere as good as Susan Fanetti's Signal Bend series. Just my opinion, though. It's obvious that biker stories are a big hit at the moment, yet not every author is skilled enough to write a really good one.<br><br>Movin’ on…</["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

<div id="review_817194146" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/817194146" />

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/817194146?book_show_action=true">Jan 08, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Christy" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Christy" href="/user/show/11284813-christy">Christy</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer817194146" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer816485768729260747"><b>4 stars!</b><br/><br/><a href='http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%206/f8c35b97-1b56-45c2-a41e-8024124b4fdb_zps9f5e5a21.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1418653394i/12864498.jpg' alt=' photo f8c35b97-1b56-45c2-a41e-8024124b4fdb_zps9f5e5a21.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/><i>It Ain’t Me Babe</i> is a MC book that’s different from most. It’s raw and gritty, it’s still got the love and romance, but the bikers/religious cult mix made it more on the unique side. I love Tillie Cole’s writing style and this was another fast paced and powerful read from her. <br/><br/><br/>This is the story of two people from two entirely different worlds. They met by chance once when they were younger and it was a day that changed both of their lives forever. Now fate has brought them back toget</span>
  <span id="freeText816485768729260747" style="display:none"><b>4 stars!</b><br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%206/f8c35b97-1b56-45c2-a41e-8024124b4fdb_zps9f5e5a21.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1418653394i/12864498.jpg" alt=" photo f8c35b97-1b56-45c2-a41e-8024124b4fdb_zps9f5e5a21.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><i>It Ain’t Me Babe</i> is a MC book that’s different from most. It’s raw and gritty, it’s still got the love and romance, but the bikers/religious cult mix made it more on the unique side. I love Tillie Cole’s writing style and this was another fast paced and powerful read from her. <br><br><br>This is the story of two people from two entirely different worlds. They met by chance once when they were younger and it was a day that changed both of their lives forever. Now fate has brought them back together again... <br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%206/9561286d-cfb1-45fb-b427-c027d5f261b0_zps5f702155.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1418653394i/12864499.jpg" alt=" photo 9561286d-cfb1-45fb-b427-c027d5f261b0_zps5f702155.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Mae has been known as ‘Salmoe’ most of her life. She is in her early twenties and grew up in a ‘community’ that is more like a cult. Being one of the most beautiful women there was not a blessing. It was a curse for her and her sisters. She went through unimaginable things, terrible things, and she got to the point where she couldn’t take it any more. She had to get out. So she did. Barely alive, she made it on the outside. Where she ended up was another ‘community’ of sorts. The Hangman’s MC. <br><br>Styx is the prez of the Hades’ Hangman MC and also known as the Hangman Mute. <br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%206/e19d6a43-5228-4bea-a5b7-fdd78d57acdf_zpsbb9806d2.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1418653394i/12864500.jpg" alt=" photo e19d6a43-5228-4bea-a5b7-fdd78d57acdf_zpsbb9806d2.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Styx has led the life of a biker. A life full of violence, sex and riding. He’s got his best friend, Ky as his VP, he’s got his Harley, he’s got his fender and he’s got girls from the club. He’s got all he needs. Until Mae shows up. Mae with her wolf eyes, eyes he’s never forgotten. That one time Styx met Mae when he was younger has been forever burned in his brain. This girl is special to him and he doesn’t know why, but he can’t get her out of his head. He wants to save her, protect her, and keep her. <br><br>But it’s not an easy transition for either of them. Styx has club business and struggles with his feelings for Mae. Mae misses her sisters and doesn’t always understand life on the outside. She makes a close friend in the MC while Styx is away on business named Ryder. He helps her to get make sense of things. <br><br>No matter what things get in there way (and there are A LOT of obstacles for these two), Styx and Mae know they are meant to be.<br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%206/1840f4bf-60e4-4782-bf86-7d58eb9eb54d_zps8b00e458.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1418653394i/12864501.jpg" alt=" photo 1840f4bf-60e4-4782-bf86-7d58eb9eb54d_zps8b00e458.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>“Styx... it is you... it has always been you...”</blockquote>
  </i>
</b> Their journey isn’t easy. It’s brutally hard, traumatic, suspenseful and heartbreaking at times. But you will love this couple together. You will root for them. There is something about boys like Styx that make me love them extra hard. He was your normal biker in some ways, but there were also things about him that were different in the best way. I liked Mae a lot too. She had been through so much and I admired her adaptability and her willingness to fight for her man and herself till the very end. <br><i>
  <b>
    <blockquote>“For the first time in my life, I feel wanted... like I finally belong. There is nowhere on Earth I would rather be than here with you. You do not cage me, Styx. You make me soar.”</blockquote>
  </b>
</i><br>Tillie Cole’s writing is fantastic. Her characters are strong and resilient. The story is unpredictable and suspenseful. It’s also got sweet and sexy moments. It’s a highly entertaining read. <i>It Ain’t Me, Babe</i> is a story that shows the power of love. Love can save you. Love can make you stronger. And love can conquer all. <br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%206/7c835dfd-67f9-4492-aa8a-4e4fd7699a68_zpsb7d20e04.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1418653394i/12864502.jpg" alt=" photo 7c835dfd-67f9-4492-aa8a-4e4fd7699a68_zpsb7d20e04.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><b>
  <blockquote>We were always fated to be together. He is my everything. He is my entire world.... Styx is my salvation.</blockquote>
</b><br></span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer881947238" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2473604177586328181">Hey all!<br/><br/>Okay, because I created this bad boy, I'm gonna give it 5 HUGE stars!!!! I'll be releasing lots of teasers too, so as I do, I'll add them on here, as well as my website, for you to check out.<br/><br/>But before all that fun stuff, I wanted to share with you why I wrote this book. Its subject matters are dark and gritty, and in parts, taboo. Many readers have messaged me to let me know how intrigued they are by the 'cult' aspect of this story and I wanted to give you some context, a reason for why</span>
  <span id="freeText2473604177586328181" style="display:none">Hey all!<br /><br />Okay, because I created this bad boy, I'm gonna give it 5 HUGE stars!!!! I'll be releasing lots of teasers too, so as I do, I'll add them on here, as well as my website, for you to check out.<br /><br />But before all that fun stuff, I wanted to share with you why I wrote this book. Its subject matters are dark and gritty, and in parts, taboo. Many readers have messaged me to let me know how intrigued they are by the 'cult' aspect of this story and I wanted to give you some context, a reason for why I chose to write about a topic quite alien to most. It Ain't Me, Babe, is very different from my usual style. Please read below, for why this book is so important to me.<br /><br />For my undergraduate degree, I studied Comparative Religion. Due to outstanding lecturers, many who were considered experts in their chosen field, I was given the opportunity to meet various people from an array of cultures and faiths.<br /><br />One of my specialised areas of study in my final year was in ‘New Religious Movements (NRM’s), Cults and Sects’. I was lucky to meet, and work with, members and former members of such religious groups. Most were happy with their lifestyle choice, others were not. I would say that ninety percent of the people I interviewed and worked alongside belonged to the former, but I will never forget the harrowing, and sometimes disturbing, testimonies and witness statements from the latter.<br /><br />Unfortunately, amongst the genuine and sincere members of some NRM’s, there are also a very small number of opportunists and individuals who, for reasons unbeknownst to most, choose to use religion, and its influence on innocent people, for their own personal gain—whether it be for power, control, or sadly, for something much more sordid. <br /><br />‘It Ain’t Me, Babe’ was inspired by the testimonies of ex-members from several NRM’s and the leaders that abused the power they had over their members—especially the women.<br /><br />The female protagonist in this novel, ‘Salome’, endures situations inspired by real events told to me personally by survivors of such groups. Addressing this topic was very important to me, as it is an area of life, of humanity, in which most people are unaware.<br /><br />Victims of these ‘opportunist’ groups are often not given a voice, and I wanted to give the many women I was so fortunate to meet, a chance to be heard.<br /><br />‘It Ain’t Me, Babe’ is a work of fiction, but the doctrines, practices and experiences of ‘Salome’, her sisters and The Order in this novel are also inspired by several brave women who chose to share their story with me.<br /><br />I am a thorough believer in the freedom of religion and respect, and have many friends, from many faiths. Most NRM’s that I worked with were honest and good people and do not deserve the bad reputation many of them acquire. What I do find unacceptable however, is when certain people take vulnerable, pure and God-fearing people and abuse their trust and kindness for their own selfish gain.<br /><br />This novel is special to me, because I was able to share some of the issues these 'opportunist cults' can create, and the scars and nightmares, survivors of such places must live with for the rest of their lives. <br /><br />The world of the Outlaw MC in this novel, however, is purely fictional, based on the author's research.<br /><br /><br />Thank you for your time.<br /><br />Tillie x <br /><br /><br />Okay, folks! Follow the links for the teasers below:<br /><br />Teaser one:<br /><br /><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://tilliecole.com/it-aint-me-babe-teaser-1/">http://tilliecole.com/it-aint-me-babe...</a><br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="2473604177586328181" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6852653-patrycja?shelf=2014">2014</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer745995793" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5829951393844204914"><b> It's live! </b><br/><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1391618077i/8420433._SX540_.jpg' width='400' height='40' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>Title:</b> It Ain't Me, Babe<br/><b>Series:</b> Standalone (for now)<br/><b>Author:</b> Tillie Cole<br/><b>Release Date: </b>April 28, 2014<br/><b>Rating:</b> 5 stars<br/><b>Cliffhanger:</b>. No.<br/><b> HEA: </b> <a class='jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction'>(view spoiler)</a><span class='spoilerContainer' style='display: none'>[ Yes.  <a class='jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction'>(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br/><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1391618077i/8420434._SX540_.jpg' width='400' height='40' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><br/>Tillie Cole is very talented writer; in my reviews of her previous books I was complementing her sweet, sassy storytelling, cute British humor and panty dropping, heart fluttering romance. Today, though, after finishing It Ain’t Me, Babe I must highlight her other values, which I haven’t gotten the chance to ful</span>
  <span id="freeText5829951393844204914" style="display:none"><b> It's live! </b><br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1391618077i/8420433._SX540_.jpg" width="400" height="40" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Title:</b> It Ain't Me, Babe<br><b>Series:</b> Standalone (for now)<br><b>Author:</b> Tillie Cole<br><b>Release Date: </b>April 28, 2014<br><b>Rating:</b> 5 stars<br><b>Cliffhanger:</b>. No.<br><b> HEA: </b> <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ Yes.  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1391618077i/8420434._SX540_.jpg" width="400" height="40" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>Tillie Cole is very talented writer; in my reviews of her previous books I was complementing her sweet, sassy storytelling, cute British humor and panty dropping, heart fluttering romance. Today, though, after finishing It Ain’t Me, Babe I must highlight her other values, which I haven’t gotten the chance to fully appreciate before now. <br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1397674370i/9309897.jpg" width="400" height="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>There is something incredibly enticing in her newest book. Not only did I feel completely taken with the exceptional plot that was fabulous roller coaster of unexpected events, but also with the characters that from the very first page were intense and so broken, my heart ached. I literally felt glued to the pages, I just couldn’t stop reading even for a second. I was so into the story that chapters just seemed to fly by. Oh boy, did I love this novel!<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1397674370i/9309898.jpg" width="400" height="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Here, Tillie showed her other darker, grittier and more complex side. Side, I was not expecting nor did I hoped for. Yet, she completely astounded me and made me her number one fan. Again.<br><br> It’s amazing how could she so effortlessly went from writing ‘butterfly in your tummy’ to ‘rough and edgy’ romances. I adore her for that and will be cherishing It Ain’t Me, Babe for a long time.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1397674370i/9309899.jpg" width="400" height="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br> <br>This story follows Salome ‘Mae’. She’s twenty three year old woman that spent all life in closed, severe commune where the rules were harsh and poisonous. When she finally realizes how wrong her people are she decides to escape the ruthless world of never really living. Barely making it out alive, bleeding out and scared, Mae is picked up by an older woman; both of them make it to Austin, where Mae is dropped near the Hangmen’s compound. <br><br>Styx is only twenty-six Prez of the biggest Texan’s MC. He’s brutal, violent and never gentle. He also doesn’t speak to any other than his best friend and VP - Ky, his father and the little girl with wolves eyes, he’s met when he was eleven. The words are stuck in his throat making it almost impossible to speak. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1397674370i/9309900.jpg" width="400" height="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>When he gets his hands on barely alive woman near the dumpster of his compound he should have let her die. Instead he makes everything to keep her alive and next to him. <br>While Mae is scarred of getting back to the hell she escaped from, Styx is in the middle of the war and having a rat under his roof. And while both of them know, that Styx ain’t a man for the fragile Mae, their bodies and hearts seem to not to listen. <br><br>This story is like no other biker romance you will find. I’ve read dozens of them already, so me being so fond of it, means that this story is worth adoring. It’s very unique and its own way beautiful. Being about outlaw MC and strict religious commune in one is not a popular or overused scheme; this is something fresh entirely. Something Tillie Cole was sure to use to her advantage in one hundred percent. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1397674370i/9309901.jpg" width="400" height="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>There were many twists and turns I haven’t seen coming. I was immensely shocked while the suspense and angst reached its limit. I would never have guessed it! I was kept on my toes till the last page and I must say that the incredible way, in which Tillie Cole mixed romance with suspense and very taboo subject of sects was a perfection!<br><br><br><i>*Review Copy was provided to me by the author, Tillie Cole, in exchange for honest review * </i><br><br><br><br><b>FOLLOW SMOKIN HOT BOOK BLOG ON: <b><br><br><a     <a title="Anovelqueen " class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/13460432-anovelqueen"><img alt="Anovelqueen " src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1504643001p2/13460432.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/3469083333?book_show_action=true">Jul 29, 2020</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Anovelqueen " class="user" itemprop="url" name="Anovelqueen " href="/user/show/13460432-anovelqueen">Anovelqueen </a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13460432-anovelqueen?shelf=bad-boys-tattoos">bad-boys-tattoos</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer3469083333" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1152798363104725028">***6 STARS***<br/><br/>I did something that I have not done in a very long time....I devoured a book. I savored each page and adored my time among the Hangmen MC. <br/><br/>River "Styx" and Salome "Mae" met as children and Styx is instantly in love and entranced by the girl with the blue wolf eyes. Years later Mae escapes from the cult commune she has been raised and abused in. She just happens to land at the compound of the Hangmen MC and is reunited with her long lost love. What transpires is a beautiful and grit</span>
  <span id="freeText1152798363104725028" style="display:none">***6 STARS***<br /><br />I did something that I have not done in a very long time....I devoured a book. I savored each page and adored my time among the Hangmen MC. <br /><br />River "Styx" and Salome "Mae" met as children and Styx is instantly in love and entranced by the girl with the blue wolf eyes. Years later Mae escapes from the cult commune she has been raised and abused in. She just happens to land at the compound of the Hangmen MC and is reunited with her long lost love. What transpires is a beautiful and gritty love story for the ages. And talk about a bad boy....Styx is it! And I love a flawed hero, someone that is not pristine and perfect. Styx has a speech impediment but still runs the MC as president and communicates his love to his woman. <br /><br />I have been drowning in droll books for almost a couple of months and I want to thank Ms. Cole for re energizing me and and helping me to recall why I love to read in the first place. When you get a novel where you are captivated from the first word until the last and you HAVE TO finish it at all costs... you have a f*cking good book! <br /><br />The characterization was varied and excellent lending to further books in the series. The pacing was perfect as you were swept away into the world of violence and vice but where true love overcomes all. It takes a truly talented author to pull off this type of book and I am so glad that I had a chance to read it. I cannot wait to read the rest of the series. Tillie Cole is now on my list of favorite authors as this is the second book of hers that I have relished in.<br /><br />I honestly cannot think of a single negative for me. Beware that it is a "dark" romance and may be offensive to some. It touches on some very sensitive subjects such as child sexual abuse, religion, psychological and physical abuse. But it made us aware of what is happening somewhere in the world right now with young girls trapped in these cults and unable to escape. <br /><br />I highly recommend! <br /><br />To read this book review and more please visit <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.anovelqueen.com">www.anovelqueen.com</a>.</span>

<div id="review_2828853185" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2828853185" />
    <a title="Giorgia ~ Reads" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/97546350-giorgia-reads"><img alt="Giorgia ~ Reads" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1597878668p2/97546350.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2828853185?book_show_action=true">May 17, 2020</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Giorgia ~ Reads" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Giorgia ~ Reads" href="/user/show/97546350-giorgia-reads">Giorgia ~ Reads</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/97546350-giorgia-reads?shelf=dark-themes">dark-themes</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/97546350-giorgia-reads?shelf=motorcycle-club">motorcycle-club</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/97546350-giorgia-reads?shelf=2020-read">2020-read</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2828853185" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4506915730362219994"><b> 4.5 Stars </b> <br/><br/>I loved this!<br/><br/>Look, sure there are things I can nitpick at. But I don’t want to, because I loved it despite those. <br/><br/><b>Is it fairly unrealistic? Sure! Did I care? No</b>. (I knew what I was signing up for, read the blurb, read the reviews and dived in, so it’s all on me) <br/><br/>Does it have trigger worthy issues? By the bucket! (<i>Child molestation, awful rape scenes - only recounted, not shown- self harm as a form of arousal, graphic murder, it’s ALL there) </i><br/><br/>Okay, so there’s one thing - the use of wor</span>
  <span id="freeText4506915730362219994" style="display:none"><b> 4.5 Stars </b> <br /><br />I loved this!<br /><br />Look, sure there are things I can nitpick at. But I don’t want to, because I loved it despite those. <br /><br /><b>Is it fairly unrealistic? Sure! Did I care? No</b>. (I knew what I was signing up for, read the blurb, read the reviews and dived in, so it’s all on me) <br /><br />Does it have trigger worthy issues? By the bucket! (<i>Child molestation, awful rape scenes - only recounted, not shown- self harm as a form of arousal, graphic murder, it’s ALL there) </i><br /><br />Okay, so there’s one thing - the use of word <b>bitch</b> as a replacer for girl/woman - <b>I know</b>, out of all the things I’ve just enumerated, the use of a word is the one to bother me! My trigger is that I cannot stand sexism and I know, again ... why do I read MC books then, you ask? I’m battling my phobia that’s why (<i>JK, the guys are hot -yeah, I'm superficial like that - and I always picture Jax Teller - not that I’d like to be a Tara, we all know how that ended.. but in my head I’ve changed that story a bunch of times and they were all a merry bunch with HEAs)</i><br /><br />Anywayyy, back to the topic at hand, the word bitch is used by every guy, all the time, referring to <b>every</b> woman, and it took awhile for me to go with it and stop it from bothering me (the more you hear them the more you realise they don’t mean anything bad by it, and I know that’s not an explanation but<b> intent matters </b>and so I’ve absolved them of their “crime” - also I’m not about to go mad about bikers not being up on their gender equality by not using derogatory names for women, cause I’m pretty sure they’ve got bigger issues. <i>Like the fact that white supremacists are carving swastikas on their chests and generally trying to mutilate them... </i><br /><br />Ok, so now let me tell you why I liked it. <br /><br />Styx is no saint, he’s not even all that amazing <b>BUT</b> I loved how obsessed he was with Mae. He had his <u>”too dumb to live”</u> moments - like that blowie he got, at the very wrong freaking time shall I add. But I truly believe he was obsessively in love with Mae so it was good enough for me. (said every stupid girl ever- <b>I know</b>, it sounded pathetic when I read it back, but he <b>was</b> sweet with her and he had this soft, guitar playing side.. yeah *swoon*).<br /><br />Now Mae, I loved her. What was there not to love. There you have this girl who hasn’t been out in the real world <b>EVER</b>, doesn’t know anything about pretty much anything and yet.. she is smart, wise, curious, assertive and so very kind. Yes, she was pretty perfect. <br /><br />Lastly there’s Rider, cause I just had to mention him and I can’t say much because .. spoilers. But damn, I was feeling all kinds of bad for him. I was there shaking my kindle and screaming “I’ll take you” ... like in the hunger games where Katniss volunteers.. except my intentions were not noble in the least (I was cured of any such temptation by the end btw - can't say why cause spoliers, but yeah, what a freaking twist)<br /><br />Hmm, what else can I add.. the story is pretty straightforward really. It’s dark, but I didn’t find it repulsively dark, apart from the scenes that recount the cult “practices”. I’ve never read anything like it and I believe that combining a cult/MC story paid off because you need to understand/have experienced messed up so that you can deal with messed up (a different kind of messed up, but still, a normal girl, with a normal life just wouldn’t be credible with someone like Styx).<br /><br />Like I said this book is not perfect <b>BUT</b> I don’t care, I was along for the ride and I totally enjoyed it. <br /><br />I’m gonna devour the next books now. I’m on a binge!</span>
  <a data-text-id="4506915730362219994" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/742766621" />
    <a title="*J* Too Many Books Too Little Time" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/9072385-j-too-many-books-too-little-time"><img alt="*J* Too Many Books Too Little Time" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1460037460p2/9072385.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/742766621?book_show_action=true">Oct 16, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="*J* Too Many Books Too Little Time" class="user" itemprop="url" name="*J* Too Many Books Too Little Time" href="/user/show/9072385-j-too-many-books-too-little-time">*J* Too Many Books Too Little Time</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9072385-j-too-many-books-too-little-time?shelf=arc">arc</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9072385-j-too-many-books-too-little-time?shelf=scorching-hot">scorching-hot</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9072385-j-too-many-books-too-little-time?shelf=happy-for-now-ending">happy-for-now-ending</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9072385-j-too-many-books-too-little-time?shelf=not-my-cuppa">not-my-cuppa</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer742766621" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16930833673772035533">3.5--<b>I Got Lost</b>--Stars!!!<br/><br/>There's a good chance this is a case of <br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380414073ra/816022.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>I just got SO LOST in the all of the details. It was too technical for my liking I think. Too many details about the Order, the Brothers, the commune, Hades, greek mythology....<br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1385564547ra/7176264.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>I think my first clue should have been the glossary of terms at the beginning of the book. <br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1390673381ra/8261001.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>The pace of this one was also really slow. Plot wise things didn't move along very fast, yet there was so much going on. Which makes no sense, I know. At times, it was</span>
  <span id="freeText16930833673772035533" style="display:none">3.5--<b>I Got Lost</b>--Stars!!!<br><br>There's a good chance this is a case of <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380414073ra/816022.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I just got SO LOST in the all of the details. It was too technical for my liking I think. Too many details about the Order, the Brothers, the commune, Hades, greek mythology....<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1385564547ra/7176264.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I think my first clue should have been the glossary of terms at the beginning of the book. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1390673381ra/8261001.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>The pace of this one was also really slow. Plot wise things didn't move along very fast, yet there was so much going on. Which makes no sense, I know. At times, it was hard to follow what was going on with the MC. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1397595783ra/9298425.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Salome/Mae has lived her whole life on this commune...it's almost a cult really. She's considered a Cursed, meaning she's too tempting to men and more likely to sway men from the righteous path. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1397595783ra/9298426.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>When Mae was 8 years old she meets River for the first time. River's father is president of the Hades Hangman MC and they are doing a drop near the commune where Mae is being held. They share a connection but River is unable to find Mae again for the next fifteen years. <br><br><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>"I'd found her too goddamn late. Hade's already pulled me into Hell. She didn't deserve to go down with me. She deserved a clean man--that so ain't fuckin' me."</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br>A tragedy allows Mae to escape the commune on her 23rd birthday. She's badly injured.....bruised physically and emotionally....when she lands at the Hades Hangman's compound and in to the hands of River. <br><br>River is now Styx, the Hangman Mute....the President of the MC. Fate brought them together again. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1397661502ra/9307588.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Mae was viewed as the freak. She was completely clueless to how the outisde world lived. Taught that everything outside of the walls of the commune was evil. She has to learn not only how to live outside of the commune but within the rules of a MC. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1385943971ra/7263245.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Styx hasn't stop thinking about Mae since that day in the forest fifteen years prior. And he wants her to be his. <br><br><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>"I w-want you too. F-fuck, I want you in m-my bed, by my side, on m-my bike. I w-want you as m-my old lady. Taking c-care of me, n-needing me...letting me inside you."</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br>Mae knows she can never be free from her past. The disciple guards will one day find her. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380405454ra/789866.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>There were some twists and turns that I didn't see coming, some that I did. The pace definitely picked up towards the end of the story. <br><br>I think for me personally, this was just too heavy on the details and happenings of the commune and the MC and not enough on the romance aspect of things. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380414983ra/818797.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>So while I got lost in some of those details, I still felt for Mae and what she had to endure at the commune. And how one chance encounter with Styx could comfort her and guide her when she needed it the most. <br><br><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>"We were always fated to be together. He is my everything. He is my entire world.....Styx is my salvation."</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br>This was a darker, more gritty read...but it was by no means dark. I liked that the story was different and unique, it was just a subject that I didn't have a lot of interest in as a whole...with all of the focus on mythology and religion.<br><br>I think a lot of people will like this one....so definitely give it a shot.<br><br><b>
  <i>ARC kindly provided by the author in exchange for an honest review</i>
</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1392695249ra/8596284.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer9415927532310936584"><br/>★★★★★ <b>5 Stars!</b><br/><br/><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>“It’s me babe... Ain’t no other man for you... but me.”</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1402091209i/9892408.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>If you haven't read this book yet, I would highly suggest giving it a try, because<br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380438071ra/885512.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Seriously. It was <b>intense, tragic, gripping, emotional, heartbreaking, and beautiful.</b> <i>It Ain't Me, Babe</i> is a story about two people from completely different worlds who formed a connection the first time they met when they were just kids. Now, 15 years later they meet again under incredibly tense circumstances but their connection neve</span>
  <span id="freeText9415927532310936584" style="display:none"><br>★★★★★ <b>5 Stars!</b><br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>“It’s me babe... Ain’t no other man for you... but me.”</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1402091209i/9892408.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>If you haven't read this book yet, I would highly suggest giving it a try, because<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380438071ra/885512.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Seriously. It was <b>intense, tragic, gripping, emotional, heartbreaking, and beautiful.</b> <i>It Ain't Me, Babe</i> is a story about two people from completely different worlds who formed a connection the first time they met when they were just kids. Now, 15 years later they meet again under incredibly tense circumstances but their connection never faded...the beauty with the wolf eyes never left Styx's mind all these years and when she shows up battered and bruised at the Hades Hangmen MC compound, he decides to do whatever it takes to keep her safe.<br> <br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1383701509i/6637626.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><blockquote>
  <i>“We were always fated to be together. He is my everything. He is my entire world... <br>...Styx is my salvation.” </i>
</blockquote><br><br>Mae and Styx were incredibly complex characters and I grew to love them throughout the story. They went through so much trouble and misery and I was rooting the entire time for their happy ending. However, neither of them were perfect and Styx made some <i>huge</i> mistakes....luckily, he redeemed himself though. Overall, this was an unputdownable and unforgettable read and I'm already anxiously looking forward to the next part of this series!<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1386461000ra/7370013.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>

<div id="review_923075679" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/923075679" />
    <a title="Glass" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4808910-glass"><img alt="Glass" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1583244629p2/4808910.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/923075679?book_show_action=true">Apr 28, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Glass" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Glass" href="/user/show/4808910-glass">Glass</a>

              <span id="reviewTextContainer923075679" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11119417897605983088"><b>2-I-have-no-one-else-to-blame-but-myself-stars</b><br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1439467596ra/15841748.gif' width='500' height='319' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>It's not as if didn't know this would happen. You'd think that I'd learn something from my previous experience when it comes to Tillie Cole. I was so frustrated after finishing <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/18105011.Sweet_Home__Sweet_Home___1_' title='Sweet Home (Sweet Home, #1) by Tillie Cole' rel='nofollow noopener'>Sweet Home</a> and <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/23262621.Raze__Scarred_Souls___1_' title='Raze (Scarred Souls, #1) by Tillie Cole' rel='nofollow noopener'>Raze</a> - I DNFed that fucker. What I expected from <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/22020052.It_Ain_t_Me__Babe__Hades_Hangmen___1_' title='It Ain't Me, Babe (Hades Hangmen, #1) by Tillie Cole' rel='nofollow noopener'>It Ain't Me, Babe</a>, I have no idea. I blame the hype. Bloody hype! And <s>fanfart</s> fanart. <br/><br/>Why I do not like this as <b>everyone else</b> does? <br/><br/>Let's start with writing. That is my issue with this author from the very start. </span>
  <span id="freeText11119417897605983088" style="display:none"><b>2-I-have-no-one-else-to-blame-but-myself-stars</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1439467596ra/15841748.gif" width="500" height="319" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>It's not as if didn't know this would happen. You'd think that I'd learn something from my previous experience when it comes to Tillie Cole. I was so frustrated after finishing <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/18105011.Sweet_Home__Sweet_Home___1_" title="Sweet Home (Sweet Home, #1) by Tillie Cole" rel="nofollow noopener">Sweet Home</a> and <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/23262621.Raze__Scarred_Souls___1_" title="Raze (Scarred Souls, #1) by Tillie Cole" rel="nofollow noopener">Raze</a> - I DNFed that fucker. What I expected from <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/22020052.It_Ain_t_Me__Babe__Hades_Hangmen___1_" title="It Ain't Me, Babe (Hades Hangmen, #1) by Tillie Cole" rel="nofollow noopener">It Ain't Me, Babe</a>, I have no idea. I blame the hype. Bloody hype! And <s>fanfart</s> fanart. <br><br>Why I do not like this as <b>everyone else</b> does? <br><br>Let's start with writing. That is my issue with this author from the very start. I have to say that it is slightly better than the Sweet Rome (I swear, I got diabetes because of that book), but still it's recognizable melodramatic and with a lot of "jungle" sounds descriptions. (If you read it, you'll know what I mean by that.)<br><br>Characters. Oh my God, characters. I hate every single one of them. Girls are Victoria's Secret models (but unaware of their beauty, or how sexually attractive they are - despite being told that they are sinners and temptation to all men all their lives). They are like virgins, but they are not exactly virgins. And boys love that shit! They go ape-shit crazy when Mae appears on compound. (And later her sisters.) Speaking about guys... Anyone watching Vikings? Yeah... They are love child of Vikings and King Kong. Plus, some Tarzan and SoA. On meth overdose. Crazy fuckers. <br><br>I feel awkward now among all you fangirls. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1439467596ra/15841749.gif" width="500" height="244" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>That's not all.<br>The story.<br>Religious cult that uses young girls, lives by crazy-ass rules and basically is lead by pedophiles. on the other hand there is outlaw biker club with gorgeous, misunderstood, lethal and dangerous men. Both "worlds" mixed in dark modern fairy tale. <br>Plus <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/41865.Twilight__Twilight___1_" title="Twilight (Twilight, #1) by Stephenie Meyer" rel="nofollow noopener">Twilight</a>.<br>I shit you not. There's straight from the book Bella-Edward-Jacob twist. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1439467596ra/15841750.gif" width="500" height="220" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Why didn't I DNFed it?</b> <br><br>Because no matter how ridiculous it is when you think about it, Hades Hangmen series is a trashy read that gets you addicted. I still want to see how will things work out for Delilah and Maddie. Flame the crazy ape number one and Ky, the whore. This is the series that will make you feel crazy and frustrated and furious at yourself because you're so weak and stupid and you cannot resist reading next sequel. </span>

        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



          <div>
    <span class="greyText">Recommended to Tears Of Venus, but humans call me Mina by: </span>
      <a href="/user/show/101308475-oumaima">Oumaima</a>
  </div>


          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/58714144-tears-of-venus-but-humans-call-me-mina?shelf=loki-approves">loki-approves</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/58714144-tears-of-venus-but-humans-call-me-mina?shelf=3-and-a-half-stars">3-and-a-half-stars</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer3488969383" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16692893933352427489"><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote> It Ain't Me Babe - 3.5 ⭐️s<br/>Heart Recaptured - 4 ⭐️s<br/>Souls Unfractured - currently reading</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br/><br/><b>
  <blockquote>“You need a st-strong man, babe. You n-n-need a man to l-love you, to pr-protect you, to be your f-fuckin’ world.” Her breath paused and I smirked. “It’s m-me, babe. It’s s-so fuckin’ me.”</blockquote>
</b><br/><b>Song :</b> <a href='https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vNy5UEpvc3w' rel='nofollow noopener'> Pistol Annies - I Hope You're The End Of My Story</a><br/><br/><b>
  <u>Warning : if you don’t like spoilers, please don’t read this, because it’s a SPOILER FEST.</u>
</b><br/><br/>This series has been on my radar forever, but I stayed aw</span>
  <span id="freeText16692893933352427489" style="display:none"><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote> It Ain't Me Babe - 3.5 ⭐️s<br>Heart Recaptured - 4 ⭐️s<br>Souls Unfractured - currently reading</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br><br><b>
  <blockquote>“You need a st-strong man, babe. You n-n-need a man to l-love you, to pr-protect you, to be your f-fuckin’ world.” Her breath paused and I smirked. “It’s m-me, babe. It’s s-so fuckin’ me.”</blockquote>
</b><br><b>Song :</b> <a href="https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vNy5UEpvc3w" rel="nofollow noopener"> Pistol Annies - I Hope You're The End Of My Story</a><br><br><b>
  <u>Warning : if you don’t like spoilers, please don’t read this, because it’s a SPOILER FEST.</u>
</b><br><br>This series has been on my radar forever, but I stayed away for so long because the MC life is just not my thing. All the <b>bitch (131 times)</b> and <b>brother (284 times)</b> and <b>load’sa (one time, thank God)</b> - ridiculous.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1597535678ra/29973718.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>But I’m glad I finally took the plunge, because let me tell you : <b>I. AM. HOOKED.</b><br><br>This is the story of <b>Salome “Mae”</b> and <b>River “Styx”</b>.<br>They met when Mae was 8, just introduced to her duty as "sister" and Styx was 11, struggling to speak to anyone besides his father and his best friend. They shared a connection, as Styx was able to talk to her (his lucky number 3) and Mae found a boy that appeared like light in the dark, giving her her first and only kiss. <br>Fast forward 15 years, and Mae is on the run from the cult, badly injured and fighting for her life. By a miracle, she ends up on Styx’s doorstep, kickstarting a chain of events none of them saw coming. <br><br><b>
  <u>➥ Styx “The Hangmen Mute”, Prez of the Hangmen mother chapter</u>
</b><br>This was me through the whole book.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1597535678i/29973719.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Styx had to talk with his fists to assert his position as Prez, making up for the fact that he couldn’t talk in front of people.<br><b>
  <blockquote>The one thing that stops people ripping on you for being a mute pussy is being a cold-blooded killer with fists of iron.</blockquote>
</b><br>He’s loyal, caring and always there for his brothers. He’s also ruthless, violent and enjoys sending people to the boatman. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1597535678ra/29973720.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>He’s been obsessed with Mae since that fateful night 15 years ago, and has been looking for his wolf eyes girl ever since. <br>Upon finding her, you’d think he’ll be over the moon, right? Well, he is. <br><b>
  <blockquote>I cradled the bitch to my chest, some possessive voodoo shit taking over my mind, body… my fuckin’ soul.</blockquote>
</b><br>But while the girl is fighting for her life, he<br><b>
  <blockquote>Turning Lois to face the wall, I guided us to the unmade bed—the bed I saved for fucking, stained with cum and sweat.</blockquote>
</b><br><i>someone please burn that mattress, please and thank you</i><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1597535678ra/29973721.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Next day, he’s all <br><b>
  <blockquote>“I-i-if you c-can hear m-me, p-p-pull through. W-wake the f-f-fuck up. I’ve b-been w-waiting on you coming back to me for f-f-fifteen fuckin’ years. No d-dying on m-me now, you hear me?”</blockquote>
</b><br>But when she wakes up, he’s convinced she’s too good for him<br><b>
  <blockquote>It killed me knowing she didn’t belong here. For the first time in my life, I wanted to do right by someone, and her being a part of this club, a part of me, wasn’t doing right by her.</blockquote>
</b><br>So naturally<br><b>
  <blockquote>I headed back to my room where Lois was already naked, eying me weird. I dragged my hands through my hair and took a deep breath. Shit! I needed Lois to fuck Mae right outta my goddamn mind.</blockquote>
</b> <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1597535678ra/29973722.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Then he goes on a month long run, leaving Mae with another “brother”, Rider, and is so shocked when he comes back and finds them super close to each, laughing, talking and being friends. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1597535678ra/29973723.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>He thankfully pulls his head out of his ass eventually, but not before an almost blowie from OW. He just got intimate with Mae and upon seeing her scars, he freaks out on her. Bitchh, why you making this about you?? She’s the one who’s been through it, ffs. After struggling with his speech <b>(my poor baby)</b>, he chooses to vocalize the classic “it’s a mistake” <b>(my poor baby is a dumbass)</b> and storms out, gets drunk off his ass and lets OW almost blow him <b>(my poor baby needs to be bitch slapped)</b>. <br>But you know what? <b>I’m the worst hypocrite in the world</b>, because when Mae gives him the cold shoulder and he turns into a lost puppy, telling her <br><b>
  <blockquote>“I-I f-fucked up, Mae. Real b-bad.”</blockquote>
</b><br><b>
  <blockquote>“I f-fucked up, Mae. I r-really f-fucked up,” I said again”</blockquote>
</b><br>I was like <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1597535678ra/29973724.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>And<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1597535678ra/29973725.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><i>come here baby, I’ll shower you with my love, you don’t need the pilgrim bitch</i><br><br><b>
  <u>➥ Mae “Snow White”, one fourth of The Cursed</u>
</b><br>Um, so, Mae. I couldn’t connect with her, sadly. For someone who’s been abused since the age of 8, been through so much atrocities and been indoctrinated since birth, she was very well adjusted to the outside world. A little <b>too</b> very well adjusted, IMO. <br>I had a sadistic fucker of a French teacher who used to hit the back of my hands with a metal tube when I made grammar mistakes, or God forbid, forgot caps in the beginning of a sentence or a period at the end. To this day, I cannot physically make any of these mistakes. And I only recently began to write in lowercase in comments and messages (only for English, I could never with French LOL). That’s me being a rebel and sending a silent lowercase fuck you to my teacher.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1510653504ra/24437782.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>but every time I do, I feel the ghost of that metal tube on the back of my hands. *shudders*<br>And you wanna tell me this girl, who’s been brainwashed since birth just let go of all that she’s been taught in the space of a month??? <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1597535678ra/29973726.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>And the sex. She’s been abused almost all her life and she jumps on Styx the first chance she got?? <br>Let me tell you a <b>not very fun fact</b>, only 40% of my aversion to physical affection is due to me being an awkward person. I understand everybody deals with trauma differently, and good for her for getting sexed up so early after her escape, but it wasn’t realistic, again, IMO. <br><br>Twice she hits the brakes during sex and I’m hyped thinking, finally some sense, but once was because of OW, and the second time because she’s afraid she doesn’t know how to please him. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1597535678ra/29973727.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I couldn’t connect with her and as a consequence, I was disconnected from everything that happened to her. She didn’t seem all that affected to me. And I hated how she didn’t think of her sisters, dreamed of saving them, just a dream. A tiny thought to them (she did once at, like, 80%? Too late, hun). But no, it’s like past Mae and present Mae are two totally different people. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1597535678ra/29973728.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>She did love Styx with all her heart, tho.<br><b>
  <blockquote>”I have only ever had one dream since I was eight. Styx, the dream is you. You stole my heart fifteen years ago and you still haven’t given it back.”</blockquote>
</b><br><br><b>
  <u>➥ STUFF</u>
</b><br><b>The Romance</b> <br>They shared a connection when they were kids, cool. But in the present, everything was not only too insta, but there wasn’t much emotional development. We know they’re obsessed with each other, but why?? By 70% of the book, they only had 4 or 5 not that long conversations with each other. In fact, Mae had more emotional compatibility with Rider. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1597535678ra/29973729.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>They spent more time together, had conversations, got to know each other, developed a friendship. He even saved her life <b>twice</b>. But again, my poor dumbass baby screamed for her so idk, I need to think on this more. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1597535678ra/29973730.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>My Expectations</b> <br>Part of my disappointment is that I thought this was gonna be about Mae overcoming her past and issues, but homegirl has got 0 issues, and this was actually about Styx getting his head out of his ass.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1512445996ra/24602302.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>What I Enjoyed Most</b> <br>➥Styx’s obsession with Mae was heartwarming, all things considered. Every time he’d describe her or what she did to him, I’d melt, even though he has a certain way with words LOL.<br><b>
  <blockquote>I’d fucked a lot of bitches in my life, done every messed-up position imaginable, stuck my cock in every hole, tried every drug, drank every whiskey, but nothing had felt quite like her tiny pale hand wrapped in mine; nothing even came close.</blockquote>
</b><br>I especially loved his obsession with her nose twitch. <br><b>
  <blockquote>I swear that fuckin’ twitching nose is gonna destroy me.</blockquote>
</b><br>➥ The club dynamic was sweet, they all loved each other (except for what they did to Pit, I’m still not over that). Every time Ky slaps Viking upside the head, I would be smiling like a maniac. <br><br><b>What Made Me Feel</b> <br>➥ Whenever my baby tried talking but couldn’t.<br><b>
  <blockquote>Work. Speak. Come on. Just talk. Anything. One word. Only one word. A sound. Something… FUCK! I tensed my chest as I tried to push the words up my throat. I could feel them lurking, mocking me, but they just wouldn’t come.</blockquote>
</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1597535678ra/29973731.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>➥ When he finally was able to talk in front of 400 people. I’ve never been prouder.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1597535678ra/29973732.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>➥ When the Hangmen showed up in the cult.<br><b>
  <blockquote>Hundreds of men, all dressed in black leather… My heart sang. It was the Hangmen.</blockquote>
</b><br>My heart sang too, ngl.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1597535678ra/29973733.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>➥ Rider's anguish. Now that is how you portray someone who's battling with what he's been taught his whole life, even though I'm not sure I buy his clueless act. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1597535678ra/29973734.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>➥ Maddie and what that motherfucker Moses did to her. <br><b>
  <blockquote>“You left me,” she said almost inaudibly.<br>My heart plummeted. I had left her alone. I, her only family, had abandoned my Maddie here, in commune, with Brother Moses, the cruelest of all the elders. </blockquote>
</b><br>And her first meeting with Flame. My heart cannot.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1597535678ra/29973735.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <u>Important Questions</u>
</b><br>➥ Why did no one regret what was done to Pit, dammit?? Poor thing didn't deserve what happened to him!<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1597535678ra/29973736.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>➥ Why is everybody in this book always snarling, roaring and twitching?? What is this, the damn jungle??<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1597535678ra/29973737.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br><b>Thank you,<a href="https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/101308475-oumaima" rel="nofollow noopener"> Oumaima</a>, for convincing me to start this series. You're an angel. 💖</b><br><br>Now, Manho Ky, Cursed Lilah and the Slutty Twins, <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1597535678ra/29973738.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>

As with most naughty books, you have to be able to leave your reality at the door – and I mean <b>REALLY</b> leave it at the door. This story is about Mae – a woman who had an <i>unconventional</i> upbringing . . . .<br><br><a href="http://lunapic.com" rel="nofollow noopener">

When she is discovered bleeding and half dead behind the Hades Hangmen’s clubhouse, club President Styx recognizes her from a chance meeting through a fence when they were just children. You know what that means, right? Instalove!!! And also a peen like no other that will help Mae forget all about her rapey past . . . . <br><br><a href="http://lunapic.com" rel="nofollow noopener">
