</a><br><br>Like I said, you have to be ready for the full blown motorbike porn experience to the nth degree with this one. But really, <b>all</b> of these stories are totally OTT so there’s not a point of no return that I can think of with regard to what plotline crosses the line to “not okay” territory. I mean hell, let’s start with the bikers. All us horny geezers get a pretty clear image in our head of what we hope to be reading about . . . . <br><br><a href="http://lunapic.com" rel="nofollow noopener">

<div id="review_1777938468" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">

    <a title="mel ☽" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/41864935-mel"><img alt="mel ☽" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1605046766p2/41864935.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1777938468?book_show_action=true">Jan 23, 2019</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="mel ☽" class="user" itemprop="url" name="mel ☽" href="/user/show/41864935-mel">mel ☽</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/41864935-mel?shelf=ow-om">ow-om</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/41864935-mel?shelf=mc">mc</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/41864935-mel?shelf=dark">dark</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1777938468" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7408895879819693336"><b>the FBI really do be giving me the side-eye whenever i read this series tho.</b><br/><br/>i can just picture them breaking into my home like this<br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1584991731ra/29154572.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/> <br/><br/>but for real... is this even <i>lEgAl</i> to write cuz there's so many fucked up things here that include children?? this series is just dark as hell that even i took a break from it for a long time but alas, here i am rereading the first three books because i forgot what happened and imma continue on with this series.<br/><br/>i honestly still liked Rider for Mae and maybe that's b</span>
  <span id="freeText7408895879819693336" style="display:none"><b>the FBI really do be giving me the side-eye whenever i read this series tho.</b><br><br>i can just picture them breaking into my home like this<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1584991731ra/29154572.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>but for real... is this even <i>lEgAl</i> to write cuz there's so many fucked up things here that include children?? this series is just dark as hell that even i took a break from it for a long time but alas, here i am rereading the first three books because i forgot what happened and imma continue on with this series.<br><br>i honestly still liked Rider for Mae and maybe that's because im biased and he wasn't sleeping with OW after meeting Mae and they emotionally connected more than Styx and i could actually see their development more but oh well.<br><br>i forgot how much of a ho Ky was and i forgot how "crazy" Flame was but i am so glad i picked this series up again.<br><br><b>reread (march 2020): <i>3 stars</i></b><br><br>* * * <br><br><i>old review:</i><br><b>original rating (jan 2019): <i>4.5 stars</i></b><br><br>It’s a good thing I know this isn’t a safe book otherwise I would’ve hated this. I usually tend to stay away from dark romances cuz they have tropes that I hate like descriptive sex with OW, explicit rape and violence and so on. I like my safe books, ya know? I just want to be happy and laughing when I read my books. Here though, it was very dark BUT I was still very entertained.<br><br>I really liked the premise here no matter how twisted it may be and maybe its cuz I normally don’t read these type of books and I have a curious mind but honestly, I’m glad I did cuz I ended up loving this and I’m planning to read the other books in this series. I’m so invested in all the characters now, I CANT STOP. <br><br>— <b>Salome/Mae</b> escapes a religious cult that’s so fuckin twisted I don’t even wanna spoil it... Let’s just say men brainwashed the women to be their sex slaves and the men are a bunch of pedophiles... ya... that’s just the tip of the iceberg. When she escapes and finally gets the taste of freedom, she finds herself in the centre of another kind of hell: the Hangmen crew.HOWEVER, she finds that the President of the biker gang is the same boy she met when she was a child. <br><br>— <b>Styx</b> or <b>’River</b> is feared by all types of gangs. This H is definitely not the type of guy u want to bring to ur parents. He loves to kill, torture, do drugs (tho he dsnt do drugs in the book it was just mentioned that he did EVERYTHING), drink alcohol, and f women whenever and wherever. He doesn’t do relationships or monogamy. but when the girl he met back when he was just a boy and has since haunted his dreams every day stumbles upon their turf... Well let’s just say it starts all kinds of drama.<br><br><b>
  <u>OW/OM Drama</u>
</b><br>One thing I REALLY hate is sex scene with OW especially right after the H meets the h<br>For the safety ppl, there’s at least <b>4 sex scenes with OW</b>: 1 full-on bj, 1 full-on descriptive sex scene, 1 fade to black and 1 almost bj (but H stops OW cuz he was thinking of h AND h catches them too)<br><br>Listen, I knew there was gonna be scenes with OW but I actually tolerated it here cuz I kinda expected it from his character. I mean he is the President of a MC sooo. It wasn’t random and out of character and 2 scenes with OW are before he meets the h and the other 2 is him trying and not trying to think bout the h. AGAIN, I really hate this (I can tolerate it tho) but oh weelllll <br><br>And the OM, <b>Rider</b>... I loved him (EXCLUDING Cain!)<br>This is the first time where I preferred the OM to the H! I was rooting for the h to end up with this guy in the beginning! I really did believe in his love for the h and it was definitely more powerful, imo. The H’s inner monologue focused more on lust and this unfortunately made me NOT believe in his love for Mae. <br><br>Ryder doesn’t whore around and do the other bad shit (other than killing) the H does AND he’s waiting for a woman he loves to sleep with her. He was good and kind and the sweetest guy to the h but she friendzoned him so bad. My heart broke for him whenever he saw the h with the H. And the scene where he poured his heart out and begged the h to run away with him? My heart literally broke. I loved him until... well, until <b>Cain</b> happened. That’s a whole other person that I will forever separate from Rider and imma just ignore... For now. <br><br>The violence here was not too bad, I’ve read more violent books like Game of Thrones and the Throne of Glass series, so I wasn’t too iffy bout it EXCEPT the parts when Flame gets aroused by cutting himself... like, EEEEEWWWW. The other dark subjects obviously made me feel uncomfortable but hey, this is dark romance right? The goal is to make readers uncomfortable in a way? Well The Order definitely gave me the creeps.<br><br>-<br>-<br>-<br><br>I really recommend this book if ur in the mood for dark romance bc this was definitely a page-turner for me 100%<br><br>I can’t wait for Ky’s book!! His should be interesting<br>AND Flame has a book too?? AND ITS WITH MADDIE?! Wtf hes a sick psycho who gets turned on by cutting himself...? <br>Well that should be interesting.</span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1084881321" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14814145038414189692"><br/><b>
  <i>** 4 "<u>you make me soar</u>" STARS **</i>
</b><br/><br/><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“I have only ever liked one boy in my life. I have only ever wanted one man to have as my own. I have only ever had one dream since I was eight. <u>Styx, the dream is you.</u> You stole my heart fifteen years ago and you still haven’t given it back.”<br/>~ MAE</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/645652.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>You see, I <b>HATE</b> cult stories. I live in <b>Turkey</b>, where religion determines the lifestyles of most people, and I have always been <i>creeped-out</i> by them. Living under strict religious rules and being a slave i</span>
  <span id="freeText14814145038414189692" style="display:none"><br><b>
  <i>** 4 "<u>you make me soar</u>" STARS **</i>
</b><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“I have only ever liked one boy in my life. I have only ever wanted one man to have as my own. I have only ever had one dream since I was eight. <u>Styx, the dream is you.</u> You stole my heart fifteen years ago and you still haven’t given it back.”<br>~ MAE</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/645652.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>You see, I <b>HATE</b> cult stories. I live in <b>Turkey</b>, where religion determines the lifestyles of most people, and I have always been <i>creeped-out</i> by them. Living under strict religious rules and being a slave in the men's world is one of my <i>absolute biggest fears</i>, so you might understand why I was shocked to see the Glossary part in the beginning of the book, explaining all kinds of weird cult jargon! When we first decided to BR this book with my bestie Sandyღ, I didn't feel the need to read the blurb, and after my first shock subsided, I resolved to give it a try even though I was scared shitless!<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1420850817ra/13278711.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Because, goddamn, <b>THIS WAS MAGICAL!</b> Who would have known that the world of <i>leather and oil and sex</i> could work so beautifully with the completely different world of religious cults. It was gut-wrenching and very hard to read at times, but the breathtaking love story made up for all the pain I had to endure... <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/7074846.Tillie_Cole" title="Tillie Cole" rel="nofollow noopener">Tillie Cole</a> once again proved to me that she is an expert storyteller! Her writing is flawless and I am obsessed with her books now.<br><br><b>
  <u>River “Styx” Nash</u>
</b> is the brutal, violent and cold President of the Hades Hangmen MC. He is the notorious <i>“Hangman Mute”.</i> He doesn't talk with words. Why would he, when he can perfectly speak with his fists anyway?<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“The one thing that stops people ripping on you for being a mute pussy is being a coldblooded killer with fists of iron. Funny how no one openly says a damn thing ‘bout choking on vocab when one smack in the mouth can paralyze from the neck down.”<br>~ STYX</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>When <b>Styx</b> finds a bloody injured young woman with long black hair and deep blue eyes next to the dumpster of his compound, he is instantly filled with the feelings of possessiveness and protectiveness. <i>
  <b>Those eyes, those blue eyes the color of a wolf’s...</b>
</i> He knows those eyes. He's been haunted by them for the last <u>15 years</u>, since that day he kissed the crying girl on the other side of the fence. <i>The girl with the wolf eyes.</i> The girl that managed to make him speak. His "number three"...<br><br><b>
  <u>Salome / Mae</u>
</b> is a "cursed". She is to be married with Prophet David and therefore <i>save the souls of all the sinners in her commune</i>. She has believed and followed the rules of her people for all the 23 years of her sorry life, but after seeing the devastating fate of her sister, she can finally see the <b>EVIL</b> lurking in the shadows of the prayers and talks of the higher power. Determined to rewrite her own fate, she escapes this prison she's been willingly shackled to for all these years and <b>RUNS</b>...<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1402256936ra/9913571.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Just when she's about to bleed to death, she is saved by strange men in black leather jackets, one of whom seems familiar to Mae. <i>The one who doesn't talk.</i> The one who uses his hands to sign. Could he be...<b>HIM</b>? The boy behind the fence? Could this man be her <i>
  <b>first and only kiss?</b>
</i><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1420851614i/13278812.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>These two exhausted me. Their road to happiness is a very bumpy one, but I think that's what makes it as beautiful as it is. I wouldn't change a thing about their story.<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>We were always fated to be together. He is my everything. He is my entire world...<u>Styx is my salvation.</u><br>~ MAE</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“It’s me babe... Ain’t no other man for you... but me.”<br>~ STYX</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><b>
  <u>Oh and guess who I liked most in this book? Even more than Styx?</u>
</b><br><br><i>FLAME</i>.<br><br><i>Yeah, that's right.</i> The brooding silent faux-hawked biker with orange flame tattoos up his neck and the word "pain" tattooed on his gums. The guy who constantly gets hard cutting himself with a blade. The guy who gets excited like a 8-year-old while watching someone get tortured. The guy with the crazy eyes and serious anger issues.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1394589608ra/8875036.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Lastly...<i><b>Rider</b>, you motherf*cker!</i> Even after all the sh*t you pulled, I still love you. I understand your pain and anger, but don't forget:<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380844587ra/3132296.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <u>So why not 5 stars?</u>
</b><br><br><b>1)</b> Because I saw one of the twists coming from a mile away, at the first 20% of the book, which was...underwhelming and a tiny bit disappointing.<br><br><b>2)</b> Because of the ending indicating with whom the other bikers of the club will be mating with. I wanted something different, but oh well...I'm sure Ms. Cole will make it work nevertheless!<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“Jesus Christ! Please tell me there’s more hot b*tches in that cell, Mae. One for each of us…”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>//////////////<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>** BR with my lovely bestie Sandyღ! ♥♥♥ **<br>Thank you so much for being there with me through this painful read babe! I wouldn't have been able to go through it without you...</i>
</blockquote><br>//////////////<br><br></span>
  <a data-text-id="14814145038414189692" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer16084931989598114647"><b>3.75 Stars</b><br/><br/><b>
  <i>"It’s me babe... Ain’t no other man for you... but me.” </i>
</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1419358105i/13045351._SX540_.jpg' width='400' height='360' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>I'm going to have to think on this one. Some things worked for me, and some things not so much. The plot was unique and for the most part, kept my interest. Honestly, I found myself loving and hating it - either I was completely captivated by the story, edge of my seat, page turning or I was rolling my eyes at the cheese being thrown at me. I felt disjointed, and I'm still not sure how I truly feel. I will say for the most par</span>
  <span id="freeText16084931989598114647" style="display:none"><b>3.75 Stars</b><br><br><b>
  <i>"It’s me babe... Ain’t no other man for you... but me.” </i>
</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1419358105i/13045351._SX540_.jpg" width="400" height="360" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I'm going to have to think on this one. Some things worked for me, and some things not so much. The plot was unique and for the most part, kept my interest. Honestly, I found myself loving and hating it - either I was completely captivated by the story, edge of my seat, page turning or I was rolling my eyes at the cheese being thrown at me. I felt disjointed, and I'm still not sure how I truly feel. I will say for the most part I enjoyed it and I am looking forward to reading more of this series.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1419359393i/13045511._SY540_.jpg" width="400" height="412" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>

<div id="review_3331859831" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/3331859831" />
    <a title="Apoorva " class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/104884953-apoorva"><img alt="Apoorva " src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1605029140p2/104884953.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/3331859831?book_show_action=true">Jun 03, 2020</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Apoorva " class="user" itemprop="url" name="Apoorva " href="/user/show/104884953-apoorva">Apoorva </a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/104884953-apoorva?shelf=books-2020">books-2020</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/104884953-apoorva?shelf=dark">dark</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/104884953-apoorva?shelf=physically-or-sexually-abused">physically-or-sexually-abused</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/104884953-apoorva?shelf=antiheroes-bad-boys">antiheroes-bad-boys</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/104884953-apoorva?shelf=3-stars">3-stars</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/104884953-apoorva?shelf=motorcycle-romance">motorcycle-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/104884953-apoorva?shelf=disability">disability</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer3331859831" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6998365236714638231"><b>Edit:</b> So I was just listening to a song and it keeps on reminding me about this book and even though the book already has an amazing playlist, I want to add this song to it because it just goes with it somehow- <a href='https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=UkxQ69mngNs' rel='nofollow noopener'>Saints</a> <br/><br/><b>I've never been fond of biker romances for a few reasons- their continuous treatment of women as objects or <i>properties</i>, calling them a bitch (it's supposedly not meant to be bad but it does sound derogatory), and their penchant for violence (o-kay,I know I like action but not witho</b></span>
  <span id="freeText6998365236714638231" style="display:none"><b>Edit:</b> So I was just listening to a song and it keeps on reminding me about this book and even though the book already has an amazing playlist, I want to add this song to it because it just goes with it somehow- <a href="https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=UkxQ69mngNs" rel="nofollow noopener">Saints</a> <br /><br /><b>I've never been fond of biker romances for a few reasons- their continuous treatment of women as objects or <i>properties</i>, calling them a bitch (it's supposedly not meant to be bad but it does sound derogatory), and their penchant for violence (o-kay,I know I like action but not without big reasons)<br /><br />But then I do like a few things too- their loyalty, their brotherhood and the familial bond even when they're not of the same blood.</b><br /><br />Okay so why am I saying all this? Because I've been unlucky in this particular trope of romance and I thought- maybe MC romance isn't for me? And it's most definitely NOT. But despite <b>hating</b> all of the things that I mentioned above-even in this book- I ended up close to liking the book itself.<br /><br />The book has twisted practices of the cult and as opposed to what we might expect, <i>they</i> were the actual sadistic bastards. The club was violent, dangerous and dark too but even they were not as bad as them, and what they did, they did openly, they claimed to it whereas the members of The Order hid it behind the false pretenses of religious BS that wasn't even true. So yeah, it was dark and bone chilling at places but mostly in cult practices. I'm seriously going to prepare myself before the next ones.<br /><br />Styx was bad and not just badass biker bad but actually bad (this is the stupidest line I have ever written I swear, bear with me🙈) He wasn't exactly upstanding and neither was anyone else. But he was <i>just so sweet</i> to Mae or as they say he was 'whipped' lol. He loved her, was infatuated with her as a young boy but at the end of the day- he <i>loved</i> her. And he played guitar, with the singing and all that.......it was sort of sweet. I liked his dynamic with everyone in the club and Mae. She was sheltered, isolated and really needed his sweet side and that's what she got. He was so rash and rude to almost everyone except her. And while I didn't like that, it was understandable because he was the President of the MC gang.<br />And I really liked Rider, I still like him a little...but all through I was sad that he didn't get love. Though I'm sure there'll be talk about that in later books, so I'm dropping it for now.<br /><br />Now, the Psycho Trio- AK, Viking and Flame. They are all worth mentioning, considering they all get books (I think) <i>but</i> the one I liked was Flame. And he was the one who scared me the most too. It was mildly horrifying (understatement) to read about him and I'm sure it would be downright torture to read his book but I'm looking forward to it.<a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ And he is going to be with Maddie (not going to elaborate, but she is Mae's sister and she was even more brutally treated than her, apparently), so it would be a fascinating thing to see how they mix up. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>Whereas I simply term AK and Viking as obnoxious lol. I'm sure they are bad but in this one, they were just.... obnoxious.<br /><br />And even if I had any unsettled feelings, this sort of shadowed it for me:<br /><br /><b>Her face melted into a stunning smile. “You spent so long telling me you were not good for me. ‘It ain’t me, babe,’ you said emphatically. Now I am perfect for you?”<br />“I was wr-wrong. So d-damn wrong. You need a st-strong man, babe. You n-n-need a man to l-love you, to pr-protect you, to be your f-fuckin’ world.” Her breath paused and I smirked. “It’s m-me, babe. It’s s-so fuckin’ me."</b><br /><br />PS: The covers of this series are really beautiful. I'm done, I swear. But <i>really</i> beautiful.</span>
  <a data-text-id="6998365236714638231" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_836166815" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/836166815" />
    <a title="Jennifer Kyle" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/9916227-jennifer-kyle"><img alt="Jennifer Kyle" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1514915429p2/9916227.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/836166815?book_show_action=true">Jan 27, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jennifer Kyle" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jennifer Kyle" href="/user/show/9916227-jennifer-kyle">Jennifer Kyle</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer836166815" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13522878218777122169"><b>3.5 Commune to Compound Stars</b><br/><br/><span>[image error]</span><br/><br/>This is the story of an escaped religious cult member, Mae finding refugee in the arms of a MC President, Styx. I think because I didn't get swept up with Styx and Mae as a couple the story fell flat for me. <br/><br/>The Hangmen Biker Club was an okay club I didn't find them any different from any other biker books. Their dealings with other organizations were broader but their compound ran the same as any other I have read. As for the commune, well I watched HBO</span>
  <span id="freeText13522878218777122169" style="display:none"><b>3.5 Commune to Compound Stars</b><br><br><span>[image error]</span><br><br>This is the story of an escaped religious cult member, Mae finding refugee in the arms of a MC President, Styx. I think because I didn't get swept up with Styx and Mae as a couple the story fell flat for me. <br><br>The Hangmen Biker Club was an okay club I didn't find them any different from any other biker books. Their dealings with other organizations were broader but their compound ran the same as any other I have read. As for the commune, well I watched HBO’s <i> Big Love</i> and The Order was pretty similar with Juniper Creek minus some of crazy ceremonies etc. <br><br>My major issue was once again... a story that wants to me to buy a once meeting between two extremely young kids that instills a bond of forever!! An eight year girl who falls fatefully in love with an 11 year old boy and visa versa from one meeting is complete bull…sorry.<br><br>Mae’s adaption to life at the compound was interesting as was Styx and Rider’s feelings for her. I enjoyed Styx’s bad ass leadership of his chapter and I guess I bought his love for “old wolf eyes”.<br><br>The convenience of the rescue right at the wedding ceremony…talk about timing. <br> <br><b>
  <i>”It is my love. He has come for me.”</i>
</b><br><br>Cain being a part of the cult and not growing up in it and completely unfamiliar with their ways but yet is the successor to the Prophet????<br><br><b>
  <i>”…I didn’t realize what they were really like…”</i>
</b><br><br>The ending with the other hot cursed girls catching the top biker’s eyes had me shaking my head.<br><br><b>
  <i>”Jesus Christ! Please tell me there’s more hot bitches in that cell, Mae. One for each of us… “ </i>
</b><br><br>Overall, I found this to be an okay read, although Rider was an interesting character and I probably would pick up his story. So go forth and check it out for yourself because I <b>LOVED</b> this author’s <i>Sweet Home</i> series and it could just be a case that I just wasn’t swept away! <br></span>
  <a data-text-id="13522878218777122169" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1135388665" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17165991804839194283"><blockquote>
  <i>“We were always fated to be together. <br/>He is my everything. He is my entire world... <br/>...Styx is my salvation.”</i>
</blockquote><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1420556782i/13238721._SX540_.jpg' width='450' height='290' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/> <br/> <br/><i>It ain’t me, babe is dark, gritty and gut wrenching story of two people from different cultural worlds destined to be together.</i><br/><br/><b>Styx</b> the infamous ‘Mute Hangmen’ is the president of the outlaw MC club Hades Hangmen. Despite his speech impediment, he is feared and respected by all. Even being a cold blooded killer, a reputation he earned to overcome his disability he has a secret! The </span>
  <span id="freeText17165991804839194283" style="display:none"><blockquote>
  <i>“We were always fated to be together. <br>He is my everything. He is my entire world... <br>...Styx is my salvation.”</i>
</blockquote><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1420556782i/13238721._SX540_.jpg" width="450" height="290" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br> <br><i>It ain’t me, babe is dark, gritty and gut wrenching story of two people from different cultural worlds destined to be together.</i><br><br><b>Styx</b> the infamous ‘Mute Hangmen’ is the president of the outlaw MC club Hades Hangmen. Despite his speech impediment, he is feared and respected by all. Even being a cold blooded killer, a reputation he earned to overcome his disability he has a secret! The one he’s been keeping since he was eleven, the girl with the wolf eyes whom he met in the woods captured his heart for so long that it became his obsession, his lifelong desire. After 15 years of nurturing his secret, fate finally brings his wolf eyed girl to his door step in the form of bleeding, bruised and unconscious Mae!<br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“Mae was mine.<br> Fifteen long years of wanting her to be mine, <br>and here she sat,<br> curled up in my arms –<br> a fuckin’ angel in hell.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><b>Mae</b> is one of the four ‘cursed’ sisters belonging to the religious commune ‘The Order’ located in middle of the woods, guarded with heavy fence having no connection to the outside world. Mae and her sisters have been abused all their lives and one night after witnessing her dear sister’s horrific death she runs for her life and somehow manages to go beyond the safety of the fence after being chased by the guards, bitten by the dog, bleeding to death only to find herself waking up to meet the boy who stole her first kiss her only kiss when she was eight. <br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"He was my only secret... <br>my biggest ever sin. <br>He had become almost like a dream to me."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote>The concept of MC book with a cult twist was quite unique and fascinating. Most of all I loved the connection between Mae and Styx. Their romance was the best part of the story, it was typical prince charming saving the damsel in distress with lot of fucked up things thrown in their way but every moment shared with them was so very beautiful. The secondary characters are to die for; they were cruel badass bikers but funny and damn protective of their club. I’m so glad most of them are getting their own stories! <br><br><b>Rating clarification</b>: Even with the great plot and amazing writing the story felt flat at certain aspects like for instance Mae has been abused, used and tormented all her life and after being taken under the wings of the hangmen she shows not sign of depression, nightmare, withdrawals or behavioral changes and for the girl who never stepped into outside world, she adjusts very well with her new found life. Instead of giving a month leap every now and then, the author could have dealt with developing her character and making it more realistic!<br><br><u>Now for the part I’m dying to say since I read the glossary </u>: <i>*RANT ALERT*</i><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[The religious cult is a whole lot of fucked up shit! I mean, what the fuck is wrong with those motherfuckers! It was insane level of brainwashing, I’ve never seen anyone degrading woman to this level like this so called cock sucking “elders” did! Every time they opened their mouth I wanted to punch their shit ass faces! “Lord sharing” my ass, grow a pair of balls and use your hands to jerk off but leave those innocent girls/women alone! Seriously if it were me writing the story I would have used at least 50 pages to describe the ways to torture/kill those sons of bitches.<br><br><b>To the prophet, elders and the bitch sister Eve</b><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1420606959ra/13244412.gif" width="380" height="220" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br> <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br><i>Buddy read with my bestie Eda♥<br>P.S: Thanks for trusting me and going in blind babe, sorry for the freak out over the glossary! Next time let’s make sure to read the blurb before diving in:p</i></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11538033-catarina?shelf=fighters-and-bad-asses">fighters-and-bad-asses</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11538033-catarina?shelf=is-getting-hot-in-here">is-getting-hot-in-here</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11538033-catarina?shelf=i-must-like-mind-torture">i-must-like-mind-torture</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11538033-catarina?shelf=the-bad-boy-look">the-bad-boy-look</a>,

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11538033-catarina?shelf=oh-the-angst">oh-the-angst</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11538033-catarina?shelf=the-alpha-syndrome">the-alpha-syndrome</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer943132586" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1523943626989257062"><b>4 Wolf Eyes Stars.</b><br/><br/>Styx is the “Prez” of the MC “Hades Hangmen”. He fell in love at 11 years old, for a girl with wolf eyes that he never saw again. For the next years he searched for her but he never found her again. But as the president of one of the biggest MC’s, he didn’t have time to dwell on that and life carried on. <br/>Fifteen years later, he and his guys found a beat up girl, full of scars. They save her life and bring her to the club only for Styx to find out that she is the “girl with wolf</span>
  <span id="freeText1523943626989257062" style="display:none"><b>4 Wolf Eyes Stars.</b><br><br>Styx is the “Prez” of the MC “Hades Hangmen”. He fell in love at 11 years old, for a girl with wolf eyes that he never saw again. For the next years he searched for her but he never found her again. But as the president of one of the biggest MC’s, he didn’t have time to dwell on that and life carried on. <br>Fifteen years later, he and his guys found a beat up girl, full of scars. They save her life and bring her to the club only for Styx to find out that she is the “girl with wolf eyes.” <br>But Mae isn’t a little girl anymore. She lived all her life in a religious cult where woman had no choice of absolutely anything and had to subdue to all the men’s, “The Prophets”, demands. She doesn’t know much about the outside world and she knows even less about the biker’s world. <br>They fall in love one more, just like all those minutes years ago, but how can love succeed when it happens between two crashing realities? <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1421534486i/13385555.jpg" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>For some reasons, books about religious cults are always hard for me to read. I don’t understand how the “leaders” are able to brainwhash a person to that point and it’s a reality that (fortunately) I don’t understand at all. I do believe Tille Cole did a wonderful job describing that reality. And it was amazing to see the colossal differences between Styx and Mae’s worlds and see Mae slowing adapting to the “outside world”. This is not a “cotton-candy” romance. It is gritty, emotional, raw and sometimes pretty gruesome. But it is, in fact, a beautiful love story and how it can grows under the most unexpected circumstances, like the outlaw who fall in love with the brainwashed cult-girl. A story you can’t definitely miss. <br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1421173399i/13334002.jpg" width="350" height="170" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br> <b>Rating: </b> 4 Stars. <br> <b>Characters Development: </b> Mae was pretty good. She was sweet, compassionate and extremely good. But I guess that’s what happens when you are raised as a 2nd category human in a religious cult. Styx was also really good. Yes, he did have his “wtf” moments, where I just wanted to beat him, but his struggles were understandable. And how he fought for Mae was very good to see. It had a great group of supporting characters, like Beauty and Lettie, and I can’t wait to read Ky and Flame’s books!<br> <b>Steam: </b> Hot. <br> <b>Sensible Subjects: </b> <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Mental Abuse. Death. Violence. Rape. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br> <b>Love Triangle: </b> <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[No. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><b>Cheating: </b> <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[There is one cheating moment. But don’t let it stop you from reading this.  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br> <b>HEA: </b>	<a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Yes. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>
  <a data-text-id="1523943626989257062" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_963832682" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/963832682" />
    <a title="AleJandra" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/25897549-alejandra"><img alt="AleJandra" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1488738602p2/25897549.jpg" /></a>

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/25897549-alejandra?shelf=bikers">bikers</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/25897549-alejandra?shelf=adult-contemporary">adult-contemporary</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/25897549-alejandra?shelf=erotico">erotico</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/25897549-alejandra?shelf=favoritos">favoritos</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/25897549-alejandra?shelf=dark-romance">dark-romance</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer963832682" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3665002800792797001"><b>
  <u>5 <i>Bible fuckers </i> STARS</u>
  <br/>
  <br/>
  <blockquote>
    <i>"The boy River had grown into Styx the man and, despite his flaws and his harshness, he was all I wanted. All I had ever wanted. I was completely consumed by his every touch, his taste and smell, and at that moment, I gave my soul whole-heartedly, to a <u>sinner</u>."</i>
  </blockquote>
</b><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1418879646ra/12933181.gif' width='500' height='260' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Hace un año my girl<b> Kjean Lara</b>, que la adoro porque le gusta la misma crazy shit que a mi. Ella me recomendó mucho esta serie y le estoy eternamente agradecida por ello. <br/><br/>OMG como me arrepentí de n</span>
  <span id="freeText3665002800792797001" style="display:none"><b>
  <u>5 <i>Bible fuckers </i> STARS</u>
  <br>
  <br>
  <blockquote>
    <i>"The boy River had grown into Styx the man and, despite his flaws and his harshness, he was all I wanted. All I had ever wanted. I was completely consumed by his every touch, his taste and smell, and at that moment, I gave my soul whole-heartedly, to a <u>sinner</u>."</i>
  </blockquote>
</b><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1418879646ra/12933181.gif" width="500" height="260" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Hace un año my girl<b> Kjean Lara</b>, que la adoro porque le gusta la misma crazy shit que a mi. Ella me recomendó mucho esta serie y le estoy eternamente agradecida por ello. <br><br>OMG como me arrepentí de no haberla leído antes. Leí los 3 libros de la serie en una semana y los ame por completo. Ahora decidí releerlos porque esta apunto de salir un nuevo libro. <br><br><b>Amo la historia, amo los personajes y por supuesto me enamore de la forma de escribir de Tillie Cole.</b> <br><br><b>➦Que tiene esta historia de diferencia a las otras decenas de libros de motociclistas???? </b><br><br>La autora estudio Comparative Religion y se nota, y mucho. Es increíble lo mucho que el tema religioso nutre esta historia. <br><br>Dejen me explico mas. <br><br>El Club se llama <b>Hades Hangmen</b>, en honor a el dios Hades. Y no solo porque suene interesante, si no porque los miembros del club realmente creen y adoran a Hades. Lo vemos en su manera de hablar, en vez de decir que van a matar a alguien se refieren como que lo van a enviar con el hombre del bote, haciendo referencia a toda la mitología Griega.<br><br>No se mucho de los dioses griegos, pero si lo suficiente para entender las referencias. Styx el protagonista también nos habla de Persephone, su historia con Hades y lo mucho que el cree en ello. <br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"Her wolf eyes drew me in. She looked like a ghost— no , a goddess—like the paintings on the wall at compound. Like the goddess Persephone, wife of Hades, the underworld God the Hangmen wore on their patch."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>Yo que venía quejándome de que en cada libro todos los clubs siempre tienen el mismo nombre (diablos, demonios, guerreros, lobos) viene Tillie y me da a los <b>MOTHERFUCKIN HADES HANGMEN. </b><br><br> <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1467346438i/19581649._SY540_.jpg" width="500" height="470" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>Me encanta el logo del Club. <br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1467346438i/19581650.jpg" width="300" height="370" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>Por supuesto también tenemos mucho drama y tragedia en la historia. La protagonista <b>Mae</b> vive aislada, abusada y sometida por un culto religioso. Y como ya lo mencione antes la autora a estudiado estos temas y se nota mucho en la forma en la que describe la forma en que funcionan estas horribles organizaciones. Solo de pensar que este tipo de casos existen en la vida real me dan ganas de llorar. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1418879646ra/12933180.gif" width="500" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1418879646ra/12933179.gif" width="500" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>La historia se basa en Mae escapándose de este culto y llega a la casa club de los Hades, ella y Styx empiezan una relación muy complicada. <br><br>Déjenme hablarles de <b>Styx,</b> es el presidente del club y lo amo con cada célula de mi cuerpo. Lo que mas me gusta del personaje es que no es perfecto, si es guapísimo, hot, un líder nato y bad ass biker, pero es tartamudo, ese pequeño detalle le da cierta complejidad al personaje que se disfruta mucho, recuerdo como lo visualizaba hablando a señas totalmente enojado, no se simplemente me encanto. <br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"The mute man with so much responsibly at such a young age, a man who already had a woman who adored him, a fact that made my heart break into a million shattered pieces."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br> <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1467346438i/19581651.jpg" width="500" height="280" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>Algo que si les advierto, la historia esta llena de groserías, usan la palabra bitch como sinónimo de mujer, y esta llena de temas de abuso, así que si eso les molesta sin duda les puede arruinar la lectura. <br><br><b>En conclusión: </b> En una semana esta serie entro en mi top 3 de series favoritas de Motociclistas. <s>Si Madeline Sheehan me defrauda con Undeserving, esta se convertirá en la numero 1.</s><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1411143642ra/11197481.gif" width="500" height="270" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>
  <a data-text-id="3665002800792797001" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

    <div class="section">
      

<div id="review_1232732283" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1232732283" />
    <a title="Penny" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/7463065-penny"><img alt="Penny" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1420145167p2/7463065.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1232732283?book_show_action=true">Jan 15, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Penny" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Penny" href="/user/show/7463065-penny">Penny</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="did not like it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">did not like it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7463065-penny?shelf=toxicmasculinity-genderoles-andmore">toxicmasculinity-genderoles-andmore</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7463065-penny?shelf=reviewed">reviewed</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7463065-penny?shelf=toxic-romanticizes-abuse">toxic-romanticizes-abuse</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7463065-penny?shelf=likereviews">likereviews</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7463065-penny?shelf=d-read-dark-romance">d-read-dark-romance</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1232732283" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6610153593679221676">There are so many things I don't like about this book, that I don't know where to start.<br/><br/><br/><u>Mae</u>: The female main character. Mae’s character is utterly <b>unrealistic</b>, nothing about her was credible. Her character development, her behavior, her thoughts, all are completely incongruous with those of an abused girl who has been forced to live her entire life within the confines of a deeply abusive sect. <b>Where are the psychological ramifications for her abuse I wonder, or the mental shock in the face of be</b></span>
  <span id="freeText6610153593679221676" style="display:none">There are so many things I don't like about this book, that I don't know where to start.<br /><br /><br /><u>Mae</u>: The female main character. Mae’s character is utterly <b>unrealistic</b>, nothing about her was credible. Her character development, her behavior, her thoughts, all are completely incongruous with those of an abused girl who has been forced to live her entire life within the confines of a deeply abusive sect. <b>Where are the psychological ramifications for her abuse I wonder, or the mental shock in the face of being expose to a completely different believe system that defies hers. Where is the adaptation, the trauma?</b> <br />In light of this, I found very convenient for the author to jump a month into the future. Skipping, this way, all Mae’s first looks into the outside world without having to show or explain her first reactions and thoughts about it. I have to say, it was quite disappointing, but seeing as how Mae was developed after that, and how she magically adapted so completely and without any trouble to life in the MC, it is perfectly understandable that the author decided to make that leap in time. In my opinion, it would have been even better for the author to have skipped at least a year in time rather than a month, because even with that month gap, she failed spectacularly to make Mae realistic and believable. <br />Also, I found Mae sad. Not that she is sad because of her demeanor and personality, but because of her lot in life and what she ended up choosing for herself. Tragic really, to escape from a cult to end up into another one of a sort. She is sweet yes, but she was severely abused, and in the end, she chose another kind of abuse, not as horrible as the first one, but a kind of abuse nevertheless. Tragically sad, not to say psychologically unhealthy, to choose to be a man's possession after what she had endured.<br />What Mae truly needed in my opinion, was to find an actual life for herself outside the club life, or religion related life, or any kind of commune like living with their own set of rules of behavioral conduct. She needed to be independent, form her own convictions, morals and believes, be her own self and find people who could actually help her be healthy inside, not to mention find professional psychological help.<br /><br /><br /><br /><u>Styx</u>: The male main character. He is a narcissistic asshole, obsessive, possessive, controlling and a <b>male chauvinistic neanderthal</b> that has nothing appealing going for him. He is unreasonable, rash, impulsive, selfish, mentally short, inconsiderate and wholly underserving. <br />Some incidents of the story that made me despise Styx: <br />- <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Once Mae had confessed about her life in the cult, about there rapes and abuse, and even her sister, why didn’t Styx offered to find the compound, rescue her sister and friend and go all avenger angel on her abusers with the support of his mighty MC club? <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> After all, isn’t he suppose to be a tough pride bicker pres?<br />- Styx reactions throughout the book towards Rider regarding his relationship with Mae are unfair, unwarranted and hypocritical. They are just another show of Styx ’s unreasonable, impulsive, jealous, shortsighted and <b>macho behavior</b>. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ I am referring to the happenings before Rider’s true colors are reveled <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br />- I just can’t bear Styx calling the woman he is suppose to love `bitch´. The bitch calling gets on my nerves every time, no matter how many MC books I read.<br /><br /><br /><u>The Romance</u>: the romance is not nice, beautiful or well done. I am not referring here to the characters background and plot influencing the romance, I am referring solely to the development of their relationship in matters of love, not situations and happenings due to the story’s sake. <br />What Mae and Styx have between them is nothing more than <b>instant obsessive love</b>. There is no development of feelings or get to know each other; there is just plane fixation towards one another without any deep reason. This is why, during most of the book I preferred that Mae stayed with Rider and not with Styx <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Obviously, I preferred that before we found out who Rider really was <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>. I knew, that was never going to be since Styx was the male MC, but it just made no sense to me a relationship between them. It did, however, made sense a relationship between Rider and Mae. Rider not only treated her much better than Styx, who was an entitled asshole, but they also had a connection, lived together for a month and got to know and care for each other. All the while, Styx was gone and the only thing Mae and Styx had going between them was the 5 seconds meeting when they were kids that left them infatuated with one another. <br /><b>The love between Styx and Mae makes no sense</b> for many reasons. But, to top it all out, Styx is a major jerk, an no matter how many times Mae says that he was sweet with her, most of what happens between them shows the oposite.<br /><br /><br /><br />I have read a few books that evolved around Motorbike Clubs. In them, is always apparent the macho mentality and degrading and abusing behaviors towards women. While reading these kind of books, I have always expected these aspects and accepted it all as a reflection of what appears an MC life is in the real world. However, it has never bother me as much as those behaviors bothered me in this book. I am not sure what is the difference between this book and the others, or if there is actually any, but I just can’t stand the sexism here, the controlling and demeaning conducts towards women in this book. I feel is just plain wrong and I am quite disgusted by it. Maybe I am just fed up with so much accepted machismo in romance books, all disguised as swoon worthy shows of love. But the thing is, this book has left me insulted and outraged as a woman. <br /><br /><br /><br />All of this is why, so many times while reading, <b>I considered not finishing the book</b>. But eventually, I decided to endure and push through all the way to the end, so I could write a complete and more accurate opinion about it. I won’t lie, it has been extremely difficult to finish it. Moments like when Mae said that Styx ended up giving her permission to work, made me want to through my ebook out the window in disgust.<br /><br /><br />P.S.: Love the cover, hate the title.</span>
  <a data-text-id="6610153593679221676" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/762027125" />
    <a title="Tessamari ♥Many Waters...♥ ~ Sweet Spot Book Blog" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4597644-tessamari-many-waters-sweet-spot-book-blog"><img alt="Tessamari ♥Many Waters...♥ ~ Sweet Spot Book Blog" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1416791332p2/4597644.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/762027125?book_show_action=true">Nov 10, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Tessamari ♥Many Waters...♥ ~ Sweet Spot Book Blog" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Tessamari ♥Many Waters...♥ ~ Sweet Spot Book Blog" href="/user/show/4597644-tessamari-many-waters-sweet-spot-book-blog">Tessamari ♥Many Waters...♥ ~ Sweet Spot Book Blog</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4597644-tessamari-many-waters-sweet-spot-book-blog?shelf=hot-and-heavy">hot-and-heavy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4597644-tessamari-many-waters-sweet-spot-book-blog?shelf=crack-books">crack-books</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4597644-tessamari-many-waters-sweet-spot-book-blog?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4597644-tessamari-many-waters-sweet-spot-book-blog?shelf=highly-emotional">highly-emotional</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4597644-tessamari-many-waters-sweet-spot-book-blog?shelf=lead-character-bad-boy">lead-character-bad-boy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4597644-tessamari-many-waters-sweet-spot-book-blog?shelf=lead-character-player">lead-character-player</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4597644-tessamari-many-waters-sweet-spot-book-blog?shelf=must-re-read-again">must-re-read-again</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4597644-tessamari-many-waters-sweet-spot-book-blog?shelf=dual-pov">dual-pov</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4597644-tessamari-many-waters-sweet-spot-book-blog?shelf=first-love-crush">first-love-crush</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4597644-tessamari-many-waters-sweet-spot-book-blog?shelf=lead-character-tattooed-and-sexy">lead-character-tattooed-and-sexy</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer762027125" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1622841298766910596"><a href='http://s1094.photobucket.com/user/thessamari/media/IAMBPic_zps08140480.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1397461188i/9278903._SX540_.jpg' alt=' photo IAMBPic_zps08140480.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><i>*Photo obtained from Author Tillie Cole's FB Page*</i><br/><br/>FIVE+++++ HUGE STARS!<br/><br/><b>
  <i>If this made me a sinner, then I was glad to be a <u>fallen</u></i>
</b><br/><br/>Ok. I honestly don’t know where to start. I’m in fucking AWE of this writer…just pure…utter…awe. I’m a massive fan of Tillie Cole, and this story just solidifies why I love her stories so much. She has taken a big risk writing this because it is extremely different from her previous work. This is <b>NOT</b> your typical MC story. Oh, no. There are so many other elements</span>
  <span id="freeText1622841298766910596" style="display:none"><a href="http://s1094.photobucket.com/user/thessamari/media/IAMBPic_zps08140480.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1397461188i/9278903._SX540_.jpg" alt=" photo IAMBPic_zps08140480.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><i>*Photo obtained from Author Tillie Cole's FB Page*</i><br><br>FIVE+++++ HUGE STARS!<br><br><b>
  <i>If this made me a sinner, then I was glad to be a <u>fallen</u></i>
</b><br><br>Ok. I honestly don’t know where to start. I’m in fucking AWE of this writer…just pure…utter…awe. I’m a massive fan of Tillie Cole, and this story just solidifies why I love her stories so much. She has taken a big risk writing this because it is extremely different from her previous work. This is <b>NOT</b> your typical MC story. Oh, no. There are so many other elements that make it stand out.<br><br><b>Please be warned</b> – This is a bit on the darker and edgier side, but that just makes it even more unique. <u>This is phenomenal!!</u> <br><br><b>
  <i>The one thing that stops people ripping on you for being a mute pussy is being a coldblooded psychopath with fists of iron. </i>
</b><br><br>The story of Styx and Salome (“Mae”) first began when he was only eleven and she eight. Styx stumbled upon Mae while his father, the president of the Hades Hangmen, was taking care of club business. He saw her behind a massive fence and she seemed very distressed. Styx, for the most part, is mute. The only persons he feels comfortable talking to are his father and his best friend, Ky. But there was something about the beautiful girl with the blue wolf eyes that made him want to try to loosen the python in his throat and talk to her. Regardless of the few words they shared a kiss and an instant connection was made between the two. However, finding her again proved to be nearly impossible.<br><br>Fifteen years later we find Mae escaping the commune. Fate then delivers her right in front of the Hangmen’s club door. Something about this mysterious woman reminded Styx of the girl with the wolf eyes; the girl whom he has never forgotten. She can’t be <u>the</u> girl, can she? <br><br>When he finds out the mystery woman is indeed Mae, all he wants to do is keep and protect her. He’s never felt a connection like this before and he doesn’t quite know what to do. As the President of the MC, he wants to do right by her. Mae is so innocent and so confused by this new world, he knew that once she finds out exactly what he does, she will be further frightened. He has no choice but to keep his distance.<br><br><b>
  <i>“I-I’ve killed p-p-people. I-I’ve even l-liked it, and” – I knew I was bringing the final death blow – “I’ll d-do it again. Y-you want someone g-g-good to take c-care of you. I-it ain’t me, babe.” </i>
</b><br><br>I was very torn by Styx’s character. I felt a lot of things for him: Love, empathy, and even frustration. The way he tried to drive Mae away was a bit hard to take. It was this decision that ultimately leads to further complications down the road, particularly when one of his MC brothers, Rider, falls for Mae himself. <br><br><b>
  <i>Styx was sin; Rider was peace.</i>
</b><br><br>Oh, Rider. My feelings for him were so conflicted. I loved him and my heart ached for him. His unrequited love for Mae was purely heartbreaking. He was entrusted with looking out for Mae while Styx was away on club business. The two became very close friends, but Rider eventually fell head over heels in love with Mae. I cried for him, but as the story progressed, the secrets behind Rider truly took me by surprise. My heart still aches when I think of him. <br><br><b>
  <i>“I thought you said, ‘it ain’t you who’s meant for me’?”<br>He laughed. He rarely laughed, but when he did, I rejoiced at the sound of it: husky, deep…male. “Oh, it’s me, babe…Ain’t no other man for you…but me.”</i>
</b><br><br>I’m a massive fan of Greek Mythology and so it was inevitable that I would be so enamored by Styx and Salome’s characters. The parallel references to Hades/Persephone were very prevalent in the story and both characters really reflected the meaning/curse of their namesake. <br><br>As for Mae, well, she was a strong heroine. As I told Tills, “she was patience, love, beauty and forgiveness personified” - regardless of the horrific things she went through at the commune. Only a woman like her could reach a man like Styx.<br><br><i>Sigh…</i><br><br>This is seriously one of the best stories I have ever read. It was just so unique and so brilliantly written. This can be read as a standalone, but the author has definitely left the door open for some more. And, baby, I’m aching for more. <br><br>Fucking loved it!<br><br>-----<br><b>
  <u>♥♥♥ FOLLOW ME ♥♥♥</u>
</b><br><a href="http://s1094.photobucket.com/user/thessamari/media/Banner2_zps7a6c719e.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379801013i/678281.jpg" alt=" photo Banner2_zps7a6c719e.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">

<div id="review_870512174" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/870512174" />
    <a title="Patty ~ Wrapped Up In Reading Book Blog" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/14302918-patty-wrapped-up-in-reading-book-blog"><img alt="Patty ~ Wrapped Up In Reading Book Blog" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1518242765p2/14302918.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/870512174?book_show_action=true">Mar 03, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Patty ~ Wrapped Up In Reading Book Blog" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Patty ~ Wrapped Up In Reading Book Blog" href="/user/show/14302918-patty-wrapped-up-in-reading-book-blog">Patty ~ Wrapped Up In Reading Book Blog</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14302918-patty-wrapped-up-in-reading-book-blog?shelf=second-chance-love">second-chance-love</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14302918-patty-wrapped-up-in-reading-book-blog?shelf=hot-alpha-male-motorcycle-man">hot-alpha-male-motorcycle-man</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14302918-patty-wrapped-up-in-reading-book-blog?shelf=mc-books">mc-books</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer870512174" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14683967111107365056">*****FOUR IT's ME BABE, STARS*****<br/>(BR with Denisse)<br/><br/>Well this one took me for a ride!!<br/>I went into it with a little trepidation, having seen the mixed reviews.<br/>The first 35% of it seemed to drag.<br/>I had no clue what the hell this story was about.<br/>Maybe it's because I kept starting the book late at night, when I was almost dead to the world.<br/>At first I was thinking this was a paranormal read, with all the biblical and Greek mythological references.<br/>But eventually everything clicked, and I settled in for </span>
  <span id="freeText14683967111107365056" style="display:none">*****FOUR IT's ME BABE, STARS*****<br>(BR with Denisse)<br><br>Well this one took me for a ride!!<br>I went into it with a little trepidation, having seen the mixed reviews.<br>The first 35% of it seemed to drag.<br>I had no clue what the hell this story was about.<br>Maybe it's because I kept starting the book late at night, when I was almost dead to the world.<br>At first I was thinking this was a paranormal read, with all the biblical and Greek mythological references.<br>But eventually everything clicked, and I settled in for this wild and crazy ride!!<br><br><a href="http://s1276.photobucket.com/user/tennyspa/media/622c2305da74df064177d03b7d8fb18d_zps6a2aa33b.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1402282843i/9916278._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo 622c2305da74df064177d03b7d8fb18d_zps6a2aa33b.jpg" width="375" height="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br>Salome/MAE and Styx were destined to be together.<br>They meet up when they are young children nearby a gated fence deep in the woods. Styx aka "River" sees this beautiful little girl with black hair and the most beautiful blue eyes, he calls them "wolf eyes", and he is immediately mesmerized by her. She is crying and a little afraid of Styx, but comes closer to the fence when he calls her over. Styx has a very bad stuttering problem. It's so bad, that he uses sign language 95% of the time. Only his dad and his BFF, have ever heard him speak. <br>Something about Mae, makes him able to speak to her as well.<br>Unfortunately their little meeting is cut short, but neither of them has forgotten the other. <br>Styx spends the next several years obsessed with the girl with the beautiful wolf eyes in the woods, and Mae holds on to the memory of the beautiful boy she met by the fence.<br><br><br>Mae lives in a bizarre religious commune, and the things that happened to her for most of her life are just beyond horrific.<br>Styx grew up in the MC lifestyle his whole life.<br>Fifteen years later, fate brings these two together.<br>Mae escapes the commune, but ends up injured in the process.<br>Somehow she hitches a ride and ends up being dropped outside the "Hangmen's" compound.<br><br><br><a href="http://s1276.photobucket.com/user/tennyspa/media/d6d06509bd072aaee2eb73dbe6932f16_zpsf43e5ffa.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1402282843i/9916279._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo d6d06509bd072aaee2eb73dbe6932f16_zpsf43e5ffa.jpg" width="375" height="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br>It was amazing how Styx seemed to recognize her, having last seen her when she was only eight.<br><br><br>I was thinking this is pretty much bull and when we learned all that happened to her at the commune, I was surprised that she was able to be with Styx so easily right from the start.<br><br><br><i>
  <b>"I have only even liked one boy in my life. I have only wanted one man to have as my own. I have only ever had one dream since I was eight. Styx, the dream is you. You stole my heart fifteen years ago and you still haven't given it back."</b>
</i><br><br><br>BUT, I did let that go eventually and there was so much action that I was very much entertained.<br>STYX was super HOT and the sexy time had my temperature rising!!<br><br><br>There are a few other MC characters that I'm hoping will get their own books. The ending pretty much guarantees there's more to come for these guys and looks like the nightmare might only just be beginning for the Hangmen.<br><br></span>
  <a data-text-id="14683967111107365056" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_913478011" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/913478011" />
    <a title="Jen" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/6049062-jen"><img alt="Jen" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1460575899p2/6049062.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/913478011?book_show_action=true">Apr 18, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jen" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jen" href="/user/show/6049062-jen">Jen</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6049062-jen?shelf=biker-romance">biker-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6049062-jen?shelf=damaged-hero-heroine">damaged-hero-heroine</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6049062-jen?shelf=contemporary-romance">contemporary-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6049062-jen?shelf=erotic-romance">erotic-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6049062-jen?shelf=kindle-own">kindle-own</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6049062-jen?shelf=series-book">series-book</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6049062-jen?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6049062-jen?shelf=dark-reads">dark-reads</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6049062-jen?shelf=december-reads">december-reads</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6049062-jen?shelf=new-adult-dark-contemporary">new-adult-dark-contemporary</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer913478011" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8423437932371099541">I decided to make some time for a quick review, as this is a series that I am in love with and can't get out of my head!! Even days after finishing this one, I still have the Hades Hangmen stuck in my brain! I know I have read a great book when the memory of it still burns brightly through out my day. I try and figure out how this one is different from the other MC books out there; because...let's face it..there are a ton. "It Ain't Me, Babe," was very dark and edgy, but even with the brutal lif</span>
  <span id="freeText8423437932371099541" style="display:none">I decided to make some time for a quick review, as this is a series that I am in love with and can't get out of my head!! Even days after finishing this one, I still have the Hades Hangmen stuck in my brain! I know I have read a great book when the memory of it still burns brightly through out my day. I try and figure out how this one is different from the other MC books out there; because...let's face it..there are a ton. "It Ain't Me, Babe," was very dark and edgy, but even with the brutal lifestyle of the MC's; the author did a beautiful job of throwing in humor and friendship to lighten it up. With the club president, (who was known as the Hangmen's Mute due to his major speech problem)River "Styx" Nash was very hard for me to like at first; but even though he was harsh; his soft side when it came to his "bitch" made it impossible for me not to fall in love with him!<br />I actually found myself being reminded of the "Black Dagger Brotherhood" books by JR Ward. When I say this, I don't in anyway mean that this is a copy cat book or anything of the sort. The men just reminded me of those sexy vampires! The VP of the club was a lot like Rhage from BDB in his good looks/long blonde hair..oh..and I can't forget that he is a MAJOR whore!!! Then there is my favorite member, and that would be Flame. He has extreme issues which consist of self-mutilation and not letting anyone touching him etc...This reminded me of Zsadist!! Needless to say, Flame became my favorite! I am so eager for his book because I just know his story is going to be beyond brutal.<br /><br />Anyhoo, I have gone on way too long all ready. There are a ton of wonderful reviews about the storyline, so I just wanted to be able to gush about how I loved this story, because I could literally talk all day about it! LOL It has been awhile since a series has caught my attention like this one has, and I am so glad that I gave it a chance.<br />Yes, I highly recommend it; but not to anyone who is not into darker themes. Some of the things are hard to take, and will not be for everyone. If you are the type to think outside the box though, then pick this book up! Your in for one hell of a ride!!! Thank you to Tillie Cole for writing such an exciting story!!</span>
  <a data-text-id="8423437932371099541" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>
